They prove almost sure convergence to locally optimal policies. Experiments in MuJoCo show improved cost performance and consistently higher reach-avoid satisfaction rates.
本文研究了随机最小成本到达-避免强化学习问题，要求智能体以指定概率满足到达-避免规范，同时最小化期望累积成本。现有安全强化学习方法难以在随机环境中同时强制执行概率性到达-避免约束并优化成本。作者提出到达-避免概率证书（RAPCs）来识别约束可满足的状态，并开发了一种基于收缩的贝尔曼公式，作为将到达-避免考虑整合到强化学习中的原则性替代方案，证明了算法几乎必然收敛到局部最优策略。在MuJoCo模拟器上的实验表明，该方法在成本性能和到达-避免满足率方面均有提升。
Towards Order Fairness: Mitigating LLMs Order Sensitivity through Dual Group Advantage Optimization
Authors: Xu Chu, Guanyu Wang, Zhijie Tan, Xinrong Chen, Ziyu Li, Tong Mo, Weiping Li
First: 2026-05-12T11:31:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T11:31:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) suffer from order bias, where their performance is affected by the arrangement order of input elements. This unfairness limits the model's applications in scenarios such as in-context learning and Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG). Recent studies attempt to obtain optimal or suboptimal arrangements based on statistical results or using dataset-based search, but these methods increase inference overhead while leaving the model's inherent order bias unresolved. Other studies mitigate order sensitivity through supervised fine-tuning using augmented training sets with multiple order variants, but often at the cost of accuracy, trapping the model in consistent yet incorrect hallucinations. In this paper, we propose \textbf{D}ual \textbf{G}roup \textbf{A}dvantage \textbf{O}ptimization (\textbf{DGAO}), which aims to improve model accuracy and order stability simultaneously. DGAO calculates and balances intra-group relative accuracy advantage and inter-group relative stability advantage, rewarding the policy model for generating order-stable and correct outputs while penalizing order-sensitive or incorrect responses. This marks the first time reinforcement learning has been used to mitigate LLMs' order sensitivity. We also propose two new metrics, Consistency Rate and Overconfidence Rate, to reveal the pseudo-stability of previous methods and guide more comprehensive evaluation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DGAO achieves superior order fairness while improving performance on RAG, mathematical reasoning, and classification tasks. Our code is available at: https://github.com/Hyalinesky/DGAO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：迈向顺序公平：通过双组优势优化缓解大语言模型的顺序敏感性
大语言模型存在顺序偏差，其性能受输入元素排列顺序的影响。这种不公平性限制了模型在上下文学习和检索增强生成等场景中的应用。近期研究尝试基于统计结果或数据集搜索获得最优或次优排列，但这些方法增加了推理开销，且未能解决模型固有的顺序偏差。其他研究通过使用多种顺序变体的增强训练集进行监督微调来缓解顺序敏感性，但往往以牺牲准确性为代价，使模型陷入一致但错误的幻觉。本文提出双组优势优化，旨在同时提升模型准确性和顺序稳定性。DGAO计算并平衡组内相对准确率优势与组间相对稳定性优势，对生成顺序稳定且正确输出的策略模型给予奖励，同时惩罚顺序敏感或错误的响应。这是首次将强化学习用于缓解大语言模型的顺序敏感性。我们还提出两个新指标——一致性率和过度自信率，以揭示先前方法的伪稳定性并指导更全面的评估。大量实验表明，DGAO在RAG、数学推理和分类任务上实现卓越的顺序公平性并提升性能。我们的代码开源于：https://github.com/Hyalinesky/DGAO。
Summary / 总结
Large language models exhibit order bias, where the arrangement of input elements unfairly affects performance, limiting applications like in-context learning and retrieval-augmented generation. Existing methods either increase inference overhead by searching for optimal arrangements or sacrifice accuracy through supervised fine-tuning with multiple order variants, often leading to consistent but incorrect hallucinations. To address this, the authors propose Dual Group Advantage Optimization (DGAO), which uses reinforcement learning to simultaneously improve accuracy and order stability by calculating intra-group relative accuracy advantage and inter-group relative stability advantage, rewarding order-stable correct outputs and penalizing sensitive or incorrect ones. Experiments on RAG, mathematical reasoning, and classification tasks show that DGAO achieves superior order fairness and improved performance, with new metrics like Consistency Rate and Overconfidence Rate revealing the pseudo-stability of prior methods.
大型语言模型存在顺序偏见，即输入元素的排列顺序不公平地影响性能，限制了其在上下文学习和检索增强生成等场景中的应用。现有方法要么通过搜索最优排列增加推理开销，要么通过使用多种顺序变体的增强训练集进行监督微调而牺牲准确性，常导致一致但错误的幻觉。为此，作者提出双组优势优化（DGAO），首次利用强化学习同时提升准确性和顺序稳定性，通过计算组内相对准确优势与组间相对稳定优势，奖励生成顺序稳定且正确的输出，惩罚顺序敏感或错误的响应。在检索增强生成、数学推理和分类任务上的实验表明，DGAO实现了卓越的顺序公平性并提升了性能，新提出的一致性率和过度自信率指标揭示了先前方法的伪稳定性。
When Simulation Lies: A Sim-to-Real Benchmark and Domain-Randomized RL Recipe for Tool-Use Agents
Authors: Xiaolin Zhou, Aojie Yuan, Zheng Luo, Zipeng Ling, Xixiao Pan, Yicheng Gao, Haiyue Zhang, Jiate Li, Shuli Jiang, Prince Zizhuang Wang, Zixuan Zhu, Jinbo Liu, Ryan A. Rossi, Hua Wei, Xiyang Hu
First: 2026-05-12T10:40:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T10:40:28+00:00
Comments: Dataset, code, and benchmark leaderboard are available at https://github.com/WillChow66/robustbench-tc-release.git and https://huggingface.co/spaces/willchow66/robustbench-tc-leaderboard
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Tool-use language agents are evaluated on benchmarks that assume clean inputs, unambiguous tool registries, and reliable APIs. Real deployments violate all these assumptions: user typos propagate into hallucinated tool names, a misconfigured request timeout can stall an agent indefinitely, and duplicate tool names across servers can freeze an SDK. We study these failures as a sim-to-real gap in the tool-use partially observable Markov decision process (POMDP), where deployment noise enters through the observation, action space, reward-relevant metadata, or transition dynamics. We introduce RobustBench-TC, a benchmark with 22 perturbation types organized by these four POMDP components, each grounded in a verified GitHub issue or documented tool-calling failure. Across 21 models from 1.5B to 32B parameters (including the closed-source o4-mini), the robustness profile is sharply uneven: observation perturbations reduce accuracy by less than 5%, while reward-relevant and transition perturbations reduce accuracy by roughly 40% and 30%, respectively; scale alone does not close these gaps. We then propose ToolRL-DR, a domain-randomization reinforcement learning (RL) recipe that trains a tool-use agent on perturbation-augmented trajectories spanning the three statically encodable POMDP components. On a 3B backbone, ToolRL-DR-Full retains roughly three-quarters of clean accuracy and reaches an aggregate perturbed accuracy comparable to open-source 14B function-calling baselines while substantially narrowing the gap to o4-mini. It closes approximately 27% of the Transition gap despite never seeing transition perturbations in training, suggesting that RL on adversarial static tool-use inputs induces a more persistent retry policy that transfers to unseen runtime failures. The dataset, code and benchmark leaderboard are publicly available.
中文标题/摘要
标题：当仿真欺骗：面向工具使用智能体的仿真到现实基准与域随机化强化学习方案
工具使用语言智能体在假设输入干净、工具注册表明确且API可靠的基准上进行评估。实际部署违反了所有这些假设：用户拼写错误会传播为幻觉工具名称，配置错误的请求超时可能无限期阻塞智能体，跨服务器的重复工具名称可能冻结SDK。我们将这些失败视为工具使用部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程中的仿真到现实差距，其中部署噪声通过观测、动作空间、奖励相关元数据或转移动态进入。我们引入了RobustBench-TC，一个包含22种扰动类型的基准，这些扰动按这四个POMDP组件组织，每种扰动均基于已验证的GitHub问题或记录在案的工具调用失败。在从1.5B到32B参数的21个模型（包括闭源o4-mini）上，鲁棒性分布极不均匀：观测扰动使准确率降低不到5%，而奖励相关和转移扰动分别使准确率降低约40%和30%；仅靠规模无法弥合这些差距。随后我们提出ToolRL-DR，一种域随机化强化学习方案，该方案在跨越三个可静态编码的POMDP组件的扰动增强轨迹上训练工具使用智能体。在3B骨干网络上，ToolRL-DR-Full保留了约四分之三的干净准确率，并达到了与开源14B函数调用基线相当的聚合扰动准确率，同时大幅缩小了与o4-mini的差距。尽管在训练中从未见过转移扰动，它仍弥合了约27%的转移差距，这表明在对抗性静态工具使用输入上进行强化学习会诱导出更持久的重试策略，该策略可迁移至未见过的运行时故障。数据集、代码和基准排行榜已公开提供。
Summary / 总结
This paper identifies a sim-to-real gap in tool-use language agents, where deployment noise such as typos, timeouts, and duplicate tool names causes failures not captured by clean benchmarks. The authors formalize this as a POMDP with four perturbation types and introduce RobustBench-TC, a benchmark with 22 perturbation types grounded in real GitHub issues. Experiments on 21 models show that observation perturbations reduce accuracy by less than 5%, while reward-relevant and transition perturbations cause roughly 40% and 30% drops, with scale alone insufficient to close these gaps. To address this, they propose ToolRL-DR, a domain-randomization RL recipe training on perturbation-augmented trajectories across three statically encodable POMDP components. On a 3B backbone, ToolRL-DR-Full retains about three-quarters of clean accuracy and matches open-source 14B baselines on perturbed accuracy, closing approximately 27% of the transition gap despite never seeing transition perturbations in training, indicating that RL induces a more persistent retry policy that transfers to unseen runtime failures.
本文发现工具型语言代理在部署时面临模拟与现实之间的差距，例如用户输入错误、超时和工具名重复等噪声会导致失败，而现有基准测试假设输入干净、工具注册明确且API可靠。作者将此形式化为包含四种扰动类型的部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程，并引入RobustBench-TC基准，包含22种基于真实GitHub问题的扰动类型。在21个模型（1.5B至32B参数，含闭源o4-mini）上的实验显示，观测扰动使准确率下降不到5%，而奖励相关和转换扰动分别导致约40%和30%的下降，仅靠扩大模型规模无法弥补这些差距。为此，他们提出ToolRL-DR，一种域随机化强化学习方案，在覆盖三种静态可编码POMDP组件的扰动增强轨迹上训练。在3B骨干模型上，ToolRL-DR-Full保留了约四分之三的干净准确率，在扰动准确率上可与开源14B函数调用基线媲美，并缩小了约27%的转换差距，尽管训练中从未见过转换扰动，这表明强化学习诱导了更持久的重试策略，可迁移至未见过的运行时故障。
RL-SPH: Learning to Achieve Feasible Solutions for Integer Linear Programs
Authors: Tae-Hoon Lee, Min-Soo Kim
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2024-11-29T07:23:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T10:39:56+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICML 2026. 30 pages, 12 figures, 22 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Primal heuristics play a crucial role in quickly finding feasible solutions for NP-hard integer linear programming (ILP). Although $\textit{end-to-end learning}$-based primal heuristics (E2EPH) have recently been proposed, they are typically unable to independently generate feasible solutions. To address this challenge, we propose RL-SPH, a novel reinforcement learning-based start primal heuristic capable of independently generating feasible solutions, even for ILP involving non-binary integers. Empirically, RL-SPH rapidly obtains high-quality feasible solutions with a 100% feasibility rate, achieving on average a 28.6$\times$ lower primal gap and a 2.6$\times$ lower primal integral compared to existing start primal heuristics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RL-SPH：学习为整数线性规划寻找可行解
原始启发式算法在快速寻找NP难整数线性规划（ILP）的可行解中起着关键作用。尽管最近提出了基于端到端学习的原始启发式算法（E2EPH），但它们通常无法独立生成可行解。为解决这一挑战，我们提出了RL-SPH，一种新颖的基于强化学习的起始原始启发式算法，能够独立生成可行解，即使对于涉及非二进制整数的ILP也是如此。实验表明，RL-SPH能快速获得高质量可行解，可行性率达100%，与现有起始原始启发式算法相比，平均原始间隙降低28.6倍，原始积分降低2.6倍。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of existing end-to-end learning-based primal heuristics for integer linear programming (ILP), which often fail to independently generate feasible solutions. The authors propose RL-SPH, a reinforcement learning-based start primal heuristic that can autonomously produce feasible solutions even for ILPs with non-binary integers. Experimental results demonstrate that RL-SPH achieves a 100% feasibility rate, with on average a 28.6 times lower primal gap and a 2.6 times lower primal integral compared to existing start primal heuristics.
该论文针对现有基于端到端学习的原始启发式方法在整数线性规划中无法独立生成可行解的问题，提出了一种基于强化学习的启动原始启发式方法RL-SPH，该方法能够自主生成可行解，甚至适用于包含非二进制整数的整数线性规划。实验结果表明，RL-SPH实现了100%的可行性率，与现有启动原始启发式方法相比，平均原始间隙降低了28.6倍，原始积分降低了2.6倍。
Skill1: Unified Evolution of Skill-Augmented Agents via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yaorui Shi, Yuxin Chen, Zhengxi Lu, Yuchun Miao, Shugui Liu, Qi GU, Xunliang Cai, Xiang Wang, An Zhang
First: 2026-05-07T12:33:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T10:25:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A persistent skill library allows language model agents to reuse successful strategies across tasks. Maintaining such a library requires three coupled capabilities. The agent selects a relevant skill, utilizes it during execution, and distills new skills from experience. Existing methods optimize these capabilities in isolation or with separate reward sources, resulting in partial and conflicting evolution. We propose Skill1, a framework that trains a single policy to co-evolve skill selection, utilization, and distillation toward a shared task-outcome objective. The policy generates a query to search the skill library, re-ranks candidates to select one, solves the task conditioned on it, and distills a new skill from the trajectory. All learning derives from a single task-outcome signal. Its low-frequency trend credits selection and its high-frequency variation credits distillation. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop show that Skill1 outperforms prior skill-based and reinforcement learning baselines. Training dynamics confirm the co-evolution of the three capabilities, and ablations show that removing any credit signal degrades the evolution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Skill1：通过强化学习实现技能增强型智能体的统一进化
持久的技能库使语言模型智能体能够在不同任务中复用成功策略。维护这样的技能库需要三种相互耦合的能力：智能体选择相关技能、在执行中运用技能、以及从经验中提炼新技能。现有方法孤立地优化这些能力或使用不同的奖励来源，导致部分且冲突的进化。我们提出Skill1框架，该框架训练单一策略以共同进化技能选择、运用和提炼，朝向共享的任务结果目标。该策略生成查询以搜索技能库，重新排序候选技能以选择其一，基于所选技能解决任务，并从轨迹中提炼新技能。所有学习均源自单一的任务结果信号：其低频趋势用于评估选择，高频变化用于评估提炼。在ALFWorld和WebShop上的实验表明，Skill1优于先前的基于技能和强化学习的基线方法。训练动态证实了三种能力的共同进化，消融实验显示移除任何评估信号都会削弱进化。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Skill1, a framework for evolving skill-augmented language model agents by unifying three coupled capabilities: skill selection, utilization, and distillation. Existing methods optimize these capabilities separately, leading to partial and conflicting evolution. Skill1 trains a single policy to co-evolve all three capabilities toward a shared task-outcome objective, using a single reward signal where low-frequency trends credit selection and high-frequency variations credit distillation. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop demonstrate that Skill1 outperforms prior skill-based and reinforcement learning baselines, with training dynamics confirming the co-evolution of the three capabilities and ablations showing that removing any credit signal degrades performance.
该论文提出了Skill1框架，通过统一演化技能增强型语言模型代理的三种耦合能力：技能选择、使用和提炼。现有方法孤立优化这些能力，导致部分且冲突的演化。Skill1训练单一策略，使这三种能力围绕共享的任务结果目标共同演化，利用单一奖励信号，其中低频趋势用于技能选择信用分配，高频变化用于技能提炼信用分配。在ALFWorld和WebShop上的实验表明，Skill1优于先前的基于技能和强化学习的基线方法，训练动态证实了三种能力的共同演化，消融实验显示移除任何信用信号都会降低演化效果。
Qwen-Scope: Turning Sparse Features into Development Tools for Large Language Models
Authors: Boyi Deng, Xu Wang, Yaoning Wang, Yu Wan, Yubo Ma, Baosong Yang, Haoran Wei, Jialong Tang, Huan Lin, Ruize Gao, Tianhao Li, Qian Cao, Xuancheng Ren, Xiaodong Deng, An Yang, Fei Huang, Dayiheng Liu, Jingren Zhou
First: 2026-05-12T10:01:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T10:01:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models have achieved remarkable capabilities across diverse tasks, yet their internal decision-making processes remain largely opaque, limiting our ability to inspect, control, and systematically improve them. This opacity motivates a growing body of research in mechanistic interpretability, with sparse autoencoders (SAEs) emerging as one of the most promising tools for decomposing model activations into sparse, interpretable feature representations. We introduce Qwen-Scope, an open-source suite of SAEs built on the Qwen model family, comprising 14 groups of SAEs across 7 model variants from the Qwen3 and Qwen3.5 series, covering both dense and mixture-of-expert architectures. Built on top of these SAEs, we show that SAEs can go beyond post-hoc analysis to serve as practical interfaces for model development along four directions: (i) inference-time steering, where SAE feature directions control language, concepts, and preferences without modifying model weights; (ii) evaluation analysis, where activated SAE features provide a representation-level proxy for benchmark redundancy and capability coverage; (iii) data-centric workflows, where SAE features support multilingual toxicity classification and safety-oriented data synthesis; and (iv) post-training optimization, where SAE-derived signals are incorporated into supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning objectives to mitigate undesirable behaviors such as code-switching and repetition. Together, these results demonstrate that SAEs can serve not only as post-hoc analysis tools, but also as reusable representation-level interfaces for diagnosing, controlling, evaluating, and improving large language models. By open-sourcing Qwen-Scope, we aim to support mechanistic research and accelerate practical workflows that connect model internals to downstream behavior.
Summary / 总结
Large language models remain opaque, motivating research into mechanistic interpretability using sparse autoencoders (SAEs). The authors introduce Qwen-Scope, an open-source suite of SAEs built on the Qwen3 and Qwen3.5 model families, covering 14 groups across 7 model variants including dense and mixture-of-expert architectures. They demonstrate that SAEs can serve as practical development tools beyond post-hoc analysis, enabling inference-time steering, evaluation analysis, data-centric workflows, and post-training optimization. Experimental results show that SAE features can control language and preferences without weight modification, provide representation-level proxies for benchmark redundancy, support multilingual toxicity classification, and mitigate undesirable behaviors like code-switching and repetition, establishing SAEs as reusable interfaces for diagnosing and improving LLMs.
大型语言模型内部决策过程不透明，这推动了基于稀疏自编码器（SAE）的机制可解释性研究。作者提出了Qwen-Scope，一个基于Qwen3和Qwen3.5模型家族的开源SAE套件，包含14组SAE，覆盖7种模型变体，包括密集和混合专家架构。他们证明SAE可以超越事后分析，作为实用开发工具，支持推理时引导、评估分析、数据驱动工作流和后训练优化。实验结果表明，SAE特征无需修改权重即可控制语言和偏好，提供基准冗余和能力的表示级代理，支持多语言毒性分类，并缓解代码切换和重复等不良行为，从而将SAE确立为诊断和改进LLM的可重用接口。
Adaptive TD-Lambda for Cooperative Multi-agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yue Deng, Zirui Wang, Yin Zhang
First: 2026-05-12T09:56:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T09:56:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
TD($λ$) in value-based MARL algorithms or the Temporal Difference critic learning in Actor-Critic-based (AC-based) algorithms synergistically integrate elements from Monte-Carlo simulation and Q function bootstrapping via dynamic programming, which effectively addresses the inherent bias-variance trade-off in value estimation. Based on that, some recent works link the adaptive $λ$ value to the policy distribution in the single-agent reinforcement learning area. However, because of the large joint action space from multiple number of agents, and the limited transition data in Multi-agent Reinforcement Learning, the policy distribution is infeasible to be calculated statistically. To solve the policy distribution calculation problem in MARL settings, we employ a parametric likelihood-free density ratio estimator with two replay buffers instead of calculating statistically. The two replay buffers of different sizes store the historical trajectories that represent the data distribution of the past and current policies correspondingly. Based on the estimator, we assign Adaptive TD($λ$), \textbf{ATD($λ$)}, values to state-action pairs based on their likelihood under the stationary distribution of the current policy. We apply the proposed method on two competitive baseline methods, QMIX for value-based algorithms, and MAPPO for AC-based algorithms, over SMAC benchmarks and Gfootball academy scenarios, and demonstrate consistently competitive or superior performance compared to other baseline approaches with static $λ$ values.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of applying adaptive TD(λ) in cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning, where the large joint action space and limited transition data make it infeasible to compute policy distribution statistically. The authors propose a parametric likelihood-free density ratio estimator using two replay buffers of different sizes to store historical trajectories representing past and current policy distributions, enabling the assignment of adaptive λ values to state-action pairs based on their likelihood under the current policy's stationary distribution. Experiments on SMAC benchmarks and Gfootball academy scenarios show that integrating this adaptive TD(λ) into QMIX and MAPPO yields consistently competitive or superior performance compared to baseline methods with static λ values.
本文针对多智能体强化学习中自适应TD(λ)的应用挑战，由于联合动作空间庞大且转移数据有限，无法统计计算策略分布。作者提出一种参数化无似然密度比估计器，利用两个不同大小的回放缓冲区存储历史轨迹，分别代表过去和当前策略的数据分布，从而根据当前策略平稳分布下的似然为状态-动作对分配自适应λ值。在SMAC基准和Gfootball学院场景上的实验表明，将这种自适应TD(λ)集成到QMIX和MAPPO中，相比使用固定λ值的基线方法，始终表现出具有竞争力或更优的性能。
EvoNav: Evolutionary Reward Function Design for Robot Navigation with Large Language Models
Authors: Zhikai Zhao, Chuanbo Hua, Federico Berto, Zihan Ma, Kanghoon Lee, Jiachen Li, Jinkyoo Park
First: 2026-05-12T09:43:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T09:43:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Robot navigation is a crucial task with applications to social robots in dynamic human environments. While Reinforcement Learning (RL) has shown great promise for this problem, the policy quality is highly sensitive to the specification of reward functions. Hand-crafted rewards require substantial domain expertise and embed inductive biases that are difficult to audit or adapt, limiting their effectiveness and leading to suboptimal performance. In this paper, we propose EvoNav, an evolutionary framework that automates the design of robot navigation reward functions via large language models (LLMs). To overcome prohibitively costly policy training, EvoNav evaluates each candidate proposal from the LLM via a progressive three-stage warm-up-boost procedure. EvoNav advances from analytical proxies with low-cost surrogates, such as small datasets and analytic rules, to lightweight rollouts and, finally, to full policy training, enabling computationally efficient exploration under effective feedback. Experiment results show that EvoNav produces more effective navigation policies than manually designed RL rewards and state-of-the-art reward design methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EvoNav：基于大语言模型的机器人导航进化奖励函数设计
机器人导航是一项关键任务，应用于动态人类环境中的社交机器人。尽管强化学习（RL）在此问题上展现出巨大潜力，但策略质量对奖励函数的设定高度敏感。手工设计的奖励需要大量领域专业知识，并嵌入难以审计或适应的归纳偏差，限制了其有效性并导致次优性能。本文提出EvoNav，一种通过大语言模型（LLM）自动化设计机器人导航奖励函数的进化框架。为克服成本高昂的策略训练，EvoNav通过渐进式三阶段预热-提升流程评估LLM的每个候选方案。EvoNav从使用低成本替代品（如小数据集和分析规则）的分析代理开始，逐步过渡到轻量级 rollout，最终进行完整策略训练，从而在有效反馈下实现计算高效的探索。实验结果表明，EvoNav生成的导航策略优于手动设计的RL奖励及最先进的奖励设计方法。
Summary / 总结
EvoNav addresses the challenge of designing effective reward functions for robot navigation in dynamic environments, where hand-crafted rewards are often suboptimal due to their reliance on domain expertise and inductive biases. The method leverages large language models to generate candidate reward functions within an evolutionary framework, and it introduces a progressive three-stage warm-up-boost procedure that evaluates proposals using low-cost surrogates, lightweight rollouts, and full policy training to avoid expensive computations. Experimental results demonstrate that EvoNav produces navigation policies that outperform those trained with manually designed rewards and other state-of-the-art reward design methods.
EvoNav旨在解决动态环境中机器人导航的奖励函数设计难题，因为手工设计的奖励函数依赖领域知识且存在归纳偏差，往往导致性能欠佳。该方法利用大型语言模型在进化框架中生成候选奖励函数，并引入渐进式三阶段预热提升流程，通过低成本代理、轻量级模拟和完整策略训练逐步评估提案，从而避免高昂的计算成本。实验结果表明，EvoNav生成的导航策略优于手工设计奖励和现有先进奖励设计方法所训练的策略。
GEAR: Granularity-Adaptive Advantage Reweighting for LLM Agents via Self-Distillation
Authors: Sijia Li, Yuchen Huang, Zifan Liu, Yanping Li, Jingjing Fu, Li Zhao, Jiang Bian, Ling Zhang, Jun Zhang, Rui Wang
First: 2026-05-12T09:38:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T09:38:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning has become a widely used post-training approach for LLM agents, where training commonly relies on outcome-level rewards that provide only coarse supervision. While finer-grained credit assignment is promising for effective policy updates, obtaining reliable local credit and assigning it to the right parts of the long-horizon trajectory remains an open challenge. In this paper, we propose Granularity-adaptivE Advantage Reweighting (GEAR), an adaptive-granularity credit assignment framework that reshapes the trajectory-level GRPO advantage using token- and segment-level signals derived from self-distillation. GEAR compares an on-policy student with a ground-truth-conditioned teacher to obtain a reference-guided divergence signal for identifying adaptive segment boundaries and modulating local advantage weights. This divergence often spikes at the onset of a semantic deviation, while later tokens in the same autoregressive continuation may return to low divergence. GEAR therefore treats such spikes as anchors for adaptive credit regions: where the student remains aligned with the teacher, token-level resolution is preserved; where it departs, GEAR groups the corresponding continuation into an adaptive segment and uses the divergence at the departure point to modulate the segment' s advantage. Experiments across eight mathematical reasoning and agentic tool-use benchmarks with Qwen3 4B and 8B models show that GEAR consistently outperforms standard GRPO, self-distillation-only baselines, and token- or turn-level credit-assignment methods. The gains are especially strong on benchmarks with lower GRPO baseline accuracy, reaching up to around 20\% over GRPO, suggesting that the proposed adaptive reweighting scheme is especially useful in more challenging long-horizon settings.
Probing RLVR training instability through the lens of objective-level hacking
Authors: Yiming Dong, Kun Fu, Haoyu Li, Xinyuan Zhu, Yurou Liu, Lijing Shao, Jieping Ye, Zheng Wang
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-02-01T08:55:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T09:00:28+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Prolonged reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has been shown to drive continuous improvements in the reasoning capabilities of large language models, but the training is often prone to instabilities, especially in Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures. Training instability severely undermines model capability improvement, yet its underlying causes and mechanisms remain poorly understood. In this work, we introduce a principled framework for understanding RLVR instability through the lens of objective-level hacking. Unlike reward hacking, which arises from exploitable verifiers, objective-level hacking emerges from token-level credit misalignment and is manifested as system-level spurious signals in the optimization objective. Grounded in our framework, together with extensive experiments on a 30B MoE model, we trace the origin and formalize the mechanism behind a key pathological training dynamic in MoE models: the abnormal growth of the training-inference discrepancy, a phenomenon widely associated with instability but previously lacking a mechanistic explanation. These findings provide a concrete and causal account of the training dynamics underlying instabilities in MoE models, offering guidance for the design of stable RLVR algorithms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从目标级黑客攻击视角探究RLVR训练不稳定性
延长基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已被证明能持续提升大型语言模型的推理能力，但训练过程常出现不稳定性，尤其在混合专家（MoE）架构中。训练不稳定性严重削弱模型能力提升，但其根本原因和机制仍不明确。本文通过目标级黑客攻击视角，引入一个原则性框架来理解RLVR不稳定性。与源于可被利用的验证器的奖励黑客攻击不同，目标级黑客攻击源于词元级信用分配错位，表现为优化目标中的系统级虚假信号。基于该框架，结合在30B MoE模型上的大量实验，我们追溯了MoE模型中一个关键病理训练动态的起源并形式化了其机制：训练-推理差异的异常增长——这一现象虽与不稳定性广泛相关，但此前缺乏机制性解释。这些发现为MoE模型不稳定性背后的训练动态提供了具体且因果性的解释，为设计稳定的RLVR算法提供了指导。

This paper investigates training instabilities in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for large language models, particularly in Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures. The authors propose a framework that attributes instability to objective-level hacking, distinct from reward hacking, arising from token-level credit misalignment that produces spurious signals in the optimization objective. Through extensive experiments on a 30B MoE model, they trace the origin of a key pathological dynamic—abnormal growth of training-inference discrepancy—and formalize its mechanism, providing a causal explanation for previously poorly understood instabilities and guiding stable RLVR algorithm design.
本文研究了在大型语言模型中使用可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）训练不稳定性问题，特别是混合专家（MoE）架构中的情况。作者提出了一个框架，将不稳定性归因于目标级黑客行为，这不同于奖励黑客，源于令牌级信用分配错位，在优化目标中产生系统级虚假信号。通过在30B MoE模型上的大量实验，他们追溯了一种关键病理动态——训练-推理差异的异常增长——的起源并形式化了其机制，为之前理解不足的不稳定性提供了因果解释，并指导了稳定RLVR算法的设计。
Does Your Reasoning Model Implicitly Know When to Stop Thinking?
Authors: Zixuan Huang, Zhixia Zhang, Xin Xia, Yuxi Ren, Jianbin Zheng, Xuanda Wang, Hongyan Xie, Songshi Liang, Zehao Chen, Xuefeng Xiao, Fuzhen Zhuang, Jianxin Li, Yikun Ban, Deqing Wang
First: 2026-02-09T07:38:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T08:51:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advancements in large reasoning models (LRMs) have greatly improved their capabilities on complex reasoning tasks through Long Chains of Thought (CoTs). However, this approach often results in substantial redundancy, impairing computational efficiency and causing significant delays in real-time applications. Recent studies show that longer reasoning chains are frequently uncorrelated with correctness and can even be detrimental to accuracy. In a further in-depth analysis of this phenomenon, we surprisingly uncover and empirically verify that LRMs implicitly know the appropriate time to stop thinking, while this capability is obscured by current sampling paradigms. Motivated by this, we introduce SAGE (Self-Aware Guided Efficient Reasoning), a novel sampling paradigm that unleashes this efficient reasoning potential. Furthermore, integrating SAGE as mixed sampling into group-based reinforcement learning (SAGE-RL) enables SAGE-RL to effectively incorporate SAGE-discovered efficient reasoning patterns into standard pass@1 inference, markedly enhancing both the reasoning accuracy and efficiency of LRMs across multiple challenging mathematical benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：你的推理模型是否隐式知道何时停止思考？
近期，大型推理模型（LRMs）通过长思维链（CoTs）在复杂推理任务上取得了显著进步。然而，这种方法常导致大量冗余，损害计算效率，并在实时应用中造成显著延迟。最新研究表明，较长的推理链通常与正确性无关，甚至可能损害准确性。在对这一现象的进一步深入分析中，我们意外发现并实证验证了LRMs隐式知道何时停止思考，而这一能力被当前采样范式所掩盖。受此启发，我们引入了SAGE（自我感知引导的高效推理），一种释放这种高效推理潜力的新型采样范式。此外，将SAGE作为混合采样集成到基于群体的强化学习（SAGE-RL）中，使SAGE-RL能够有效将SAGE发现的高效推理模式融入标准pass@1推理，显著提升了LRMs在多个具有挑战性的数学基准上的推理准确性和效率。

The paper investigates the inefficiency of long chains of thought in large reasoning models, which often cause redundancy and delays without improving accuracy. The authors discover that these models implicitly know when to stop reasoning, but this ability is hidden by current sampling methods. They propose SAGE, a self-aware sampling paradigm that unlocks efficient reasoning, and integrate it into group-based reinforcement learning to create SAGE-RL. Experimental results on mathematical benchmarks show that SAGE-RL significantly enhances both reasoning accuracy and efficiency during standard inference.
该论文研究了大型推理模型中长思维链的低效问题，这种冗余常导致延迟且不提升准确性。作者发现模型隐式知道何时停止推理，但当前采样方法掩盖了这一能力。他们提出SAGE，一种自我感知的采样范式以释放高效推理潜力，并将其融入群体强化学习形成SAGE-RL。在多个数学基准上的实验表明，SAGE-RL在标准推理中显著提升了推理准确性和效率。
Entropy Polarity in Reinforcement Fine-Tuning: Direction, Asymmetry, and Control
Authors: Jiazheng Zhang, Ziche Fu, Junrui Shen, Yunbin Zhao, Yunke Zhang, Zhiheng Xi, Long Ma, Chenxin An, Zhihao Zhang, Shichun Liu, Dingwei Zhu, Shihan Dou, Shaofan Liu, Han Li, Wiggin Zhou, Aiden Adams, Tao Gui, Fei Huang, Qi Zhang, Xuanjing Huang
First: 2026-05-12T08:47:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T08:47:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Policy entropy has emerged as a fundamental measure for understanding and controlling exploration in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for LLMs. However, existing entropy-aware methods mainly regulate entropy through global objectives, while the token-level mechanism by which sampled policy updates reshape policy entropy remains underexplored. In this work, we develop a theoretical framework of entropy mechanics in RLVR. Our analysis yields a first-order approximation of the entropy change, giving rise to entropy polarity, a signed token-level quantity that predicts how much a sampled update expands or contracts entropy. This analysis further reveals a structural asymmetry: reinforcing frequent high-probability tokens triggers contraction tendencies, whereas expansive tendencies typically require lower-probability samples or stronger distributional correction. Empirically, we show that entropy polarity reliably predicts entropy changes, and that positive and negative polarity branches play complementary roles in preserving exploration while strengthening exploitation. Building on these insights, we propose Polarity-Aware Policy Optimization (PAPO), which preserves both polarity branches and implements entropy control through advantage reweighting. With the empirical entropy trajectory as an online phase signal, PAPO adaptively reallocates optimization pressure between entropy-expanding and entropy-contracting updates. Experiments on mathematical reasoning and agentic benchmarks show that PAPO consistently outperforms competitive baselines, while delivering superior training efficiency and substantial reward improvements.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces a theoretical framework called entropy mechanics to analyze how policy updates affect entropy in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards for large language models. The authors derive a first-order approximation of entropy change, defining entropy polarity as a token-level signed quantity that predicts whether a sampled update expands or contracts entropy, revealing a structural asymmetry where reinforcing high-probability tokens tends to contract entropy while lower-probability samples expand it. Empirically, entropy polarity reliably predicts entropy changes, and the positive and negative branches play complementary roles in balancing exploration and exploitation. Building on these insights, the authors propose Polarity-Aware Policy Optimization (PAPO), which adaptively reallocates optimization pressure between entropy-expanding and entropy-contracting updates using the empirical entropy trajectory as an online signal. Experiments on mathematical reasoning and agentic benchmarks show that PAPO consistently outperforms competitive baselines, achieving superior training efficiency and substantial reward improvements.
该论文提出了一个名为熵力学的理论框架，用于分析在基于可验证奖励的强化学习中，策略更新如何影响大语言模型的熵。作者推导出熵变化的一阶近似，定义了熵极性作为令牌级别的带符号量，用于预测采样更新是扩大还是收缩熵，并揭示了结构性不对称性：强化高频高概率令牌倾向于收缩熵，而低概率样本则倾向于扩大熵。实验表明，熵极性可靠地预测熵变化，正负极性分支在平衡探索与利用中发挥互补作用。基于这些见解，作者提出了极性感知策略优化（PAPO），该方法利用经验熵轨迹作为在线信号，自适应地在熵扩大和熵收缩更新之间重新分配优化压力。在数学推理和智能体基准测试上的实验显示，PAPO持续优于竞争基线，实现了更高的训练效率和显著奖励提升。
Federated Client Selection under Partial Visibility: A POMDP Approach with Spatio-Temporal Attention
Authors: Qijun Hou, Yuchen Shi, Pingyi Fan, Khaled B. Letaief
First: 2026-05-12T08:28:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T08:28:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Federated learning relies on effective client selection to alleviate the performance degradation caused by data heterogeneity. Most existing methods assume full visibility of all clients at each communication round. However, in large-scale or edge-based deployments, the server can only access a subset of clients due to communication, mobility, or availability constraints, resulting in partial visibility where only a subset of clients is observable for aggregation in each communication round. In this paper, we formulate federated client selection under partial visibility as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) and propose a Spatial-Temporal attention-based reinforcement learning framework. By integrating historical global models and client identity embeddings, the proposed method captures both the temporal contexts of training and the persistent characteristics of clients. Experimental results across multiple datasets demonstrate that our approach achieves superior performance compared to existing baselines in heterogeneous and partially visible settings, validating its effectiveness in addressing the challenges of incomplete observations in practical federated learning systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：部分可见性下的联邦客户端选择：基于时空注意力的POMDP方法
联邦学习依赖有效的客户端选择来缓解数据异构性导致的性能下降。现有方法大多假设每轮通信中所有客户端完全可见。然而，在大规模或边缘部署场景中，服务器因通信、移动性或可用性限制仅能访问部分客户端，导致每轮通信中仅部分客户端可被观测用于聚合，形成部分可见性。本文将该问题建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP），并提出基于时空注意力的强化学习框架。通过整合历史全局模型与客户端身份嵌入，该方法同时捕获训练的时间上下文与客户端的持久特征。跨多个数据集的实验表明，在异构且部分可见的设置下，本方法相较于现有基线取得了更优性能，验证了其在解决实际联邦学习系统中不完整观测挑战方面的有效性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of client selection in federated learning under partial visibility, where the server can only observe a subset of clients each round due to constraints like communication or mobility. The authors formulate the problem as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) and propose a reinforcement learning framework with spatio-temporal attention, which integrates historical global models and client identity embeddings to capture temporal training contexts and persistent client characteristics. Experimental results on multiple datasets show that the proposed method outperforms existing baselines in heterogeneous and partially visible settings, demonstrating its effectiveness for practical federated learning systems with incomplete observations.
本文针对联邦学习中部分可见性下的客户端选择问题，即服务器因通信、移动性或可用性限制每轮只能观察到部分客户端，将其建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP），并提出一种基于时空注意力的强化学习框架。该方法通过整合历史全局模型和客户端身份嵌入，捕捉训练的时间上下文和客户端的持久特征。在多个数据集上的实验结果表明，该方法在异构和部分可见场景下优于现有基线，验证了其应对实际联邦学习系统中不完整观测挑战的有效性。
Block-R1: Rethinking the Role of Block Size in Multi-domain Reinforcement Learning for Diffusion Large Language Models
Authors: Yan Jiang, Ruihong Qiu, Zi Huang
Venue: NeurIPS 2026
First: 2026-05-12T08:09:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T08:09:42+00:00
Comments: NeurIPS 2026 Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recently, reinforcement learning (RL) has been widely applied during post-training for diffusion large language models (dLLMs) to enhance reasoning with block-wise semi-autoregressive generation. Block size has therefore become a vital factor in dLLMs, since it determines the parallel decoding granularity and affects the rollout trajectories during RL optimisation, e.g., GRPO. Instead of investigating the effect of block size during inference on individual domains, this paper studies block size from a domain conflict perspective for dLLM RL post-training in multi-domain scenarios. The main contributions are: (1) a formulation of domain block size conflict in multi-domain RL for dLLMs, which will largely affect the post-training effectiveness for rollout-based RL methods; (2) a novel dataset, Block-R1-41K is constructed with a best-improved training block size for each sample, which also induces a Block Size Conflict Score to quantitatively measure the domain conflict; (3) a new benchmark, Block-R1, for flexible RL post-training for dLLMs in both single and cross domain; and (4) a simple yet powerful cross-domain post-training method with sample-level best-improved training block sizes. Extensive experiments on 13 distinct datasets, 7 latest RL algorithms, and various different dLLM backbones are covered in Block-R1. The benchmark is open-sourced at https://github.com/YanJiangJerry/Block-R1, with the dataset released at https://huggingface.co/datasets/dLLM-R1/Block-R1-41K.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Block-R1：重新审视块大小在扩散大语言模型多域强化学习中的作用
近期，强化学习（RL）被广泛应用于扩散大语言模型（dLLMs）的后训练阶段，通过块级半自回归生成来增强推理能力。块大小因此成为dLLMs的关键因素，因为它决定了并行解码粒度，并影响RL优化（如GRPO）中的轨迹展开。本文并非研究推理阶段块大小在单个领域的影响，而是从领域冲突角度探讨dLLMs在多域场景下RL后训练中的块大小问题。主要贡献包括：（1）形式化定义了dLLMs多域RL中的领域块大小冲突，该冲突将显著影响基于轨迹展开的RL方法的后训练效果；（2）构建了新型数据集Block-R1-41K，为每个样本提供最佳改进训练块大小，并引入块大小冲突分数以定量衡量领域冲突；（3）提出新基准Block-R1，支持dLLMs在单域和跨域场景下的灵活RL后训练；（4）提出一种简单而强大的跨域后训练方法，采用样本级最佳改进训练块大小。Block-R1在13个不同数据集、7种最新RL算法及多种dLLM骨干网络上进行了广泛实验。该基准已开源至https://github.com/YanJiangJerry/Block-R1，数据集发布于https://huggingface.co/datasets/dLLM-R1/Block-R1-41K。
CaC: Advancing Video Reward Models via Hierarchical Spatiotemporal Concentrating
Authors: Jiyuan Wang, Huan Ouyang, Jiuzhou Lin, Chunyu Lin, Dewen Fan, Boheng Zhang, Haonan Fan, Fei Zuo, Jia Sun, Huaiqing Wang, Honglie Wang, Yiyang Fan, Zhenlong Yuan, Zijun Li, Yongrui Heng, Guosheng Lin, Fan Yang, Tingting Gao
First: 2026-05-12T08:08:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T08:08:33+00:00
Comments: 27 pages, 10 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we propose Concentrate and Concentrate (CaC), a coarse-to-fine anomaly reward model based on Vision-Language Models. During inference, it first conducts a global temporal scan to anchor anomalous time windows, then performs fine-grained spatial grounding within the localized interval, and finally derives robust judgments via structured spatiotemporal Chain-of-Thought reasoning. To equip the model with these capabilities, we construct the first large-scale generated video anomaly dataset with per-frame bounding-box annotations, temporal anomaly windows, and fine-grained attribution labels. Building on this dataset, we design a three-stage progressive training paradigm. The model initially learns spatial and temporal anchoring through single- and multi-frame supervised fine-tuning, and then is optimized by a reinforcement learning strategy based on two-turn Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). Beyond conventional accuracy rewards, we introduce Temporal and Spatial IoU rewards to supervise the intermediate localization process, effectively guiding the model toward more grounded and interpretable spatiotemporal reasoning. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CaC can stably concentrate on subtle anomalies, achieving a 25.7% accuracy improvement on fine-grained anomaly benchmarks and, when used as a reward signal, CaC reduces generated-video anomalies by 11.7% while improving overall video quality.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CaC：通过层次化时空聚焦推进视频奖励模型
本文提出CaC（聚焦再聚焦），一种基于视觉语言模型的由粗到细异常奖励模型。推理时，它首先进行全局时间扫描以锚定异常时间窗口，然后在局部区间内进行细粒度空间定位，最后通过结构化时空思维链推理得出稳健判断。为使模型具备这些能力，我们构建了首个大规模生成视频异常数据集，包含逐帧边界框标注、时间异常窗口和细粒度归因标签。基于该数据集，我们设计了三阶段渐进式训练范式：模型先通过单帧和多帧监督微调学习空间与时间锚定，再通过基于两轮组相对策略优化（GRPO）的强化学习策略进行优化。除传统准确率奖励外，我们引入时间IoU和空间IoU奖励来监督中间定位过程，有效引导模型进行更扎实、可解释的时空推理。大量实验表明，CaC能稳定聚焦于细微异常，在细粒度异常基准上准确率提升25.7%；作为奖励信号时，CaC使生成视频异常减少11.7%，同时提升整体视频质量。
Offline Constrained Reinforcement Learning under Partial Data Coverage
Authors: Seokmin Ko, Ambuj Tewari, Kihyuk Hong
First: 2025-05-23T06:00:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T07:45:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study offline constrained reinforcement learning with general function approximation in discounted constrained Markov decision processes. Prior methods either require full data coverage for evaluating intermediate policies, lack oracle efficiency, or requires the knowledge of data-generating distribution for policy extraction. We propose PDOCRL, an oracle-efficient primal-dual algorithm based on a decomposed linear-programming formulation that makes the policy an explicit optimization variable. This avoids policy extraction that requires the knowledge of data-generating distribution, and only uses standard policy-optimization, online linear-optimization, and linear-minimization oracles. We show that saddle-point formulations using general function approximation can have spurious saddle points even when an optimal solution is realizable, and identify a stronger realizability condition under which every restricted saddle point is optimal. Under this condition and partial coverage of an optimal policy, PDOCRL returns a near-optimal, near-feasible policy with a \(\widetilde{\mathcal O}(ε^{-2})\) sample guarantee, without access to the data-generating distribution. Empirically, PDOCRL is competitive with strong baselines on standard offline constrained RL benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：部分数据覆盖下的离线约束强化学习
我们研究在折扣约束马尔可夫决策过程中，使用通用函数逼近的离线约束强化学习。先前的方法要么需要完整的数据覆盖来评估中间策略，要么缺乏预言机效率，要么需要知道数据生成分布来进行策略提取。我们提出PDOCRL，一种基于分解线性规划公式的预言机高效原始-对偶算法，该公式将策略作为显式优化变量。这避免了需要知道数据生成分布的策略提取，并且仅使用标准策略优化、在线线性优化和线性最小化预言机。我们表明，使用通用函数逼近的鞍点公式可能存在虚假鞍点，即使最优解是可实现的，并识别出一个更强的可实现性条件，在该条件下每个受限鞍点都是最优的。在此条件下以及最优策略的部分覆盖下，PDOCRL返回一个近最优、近可行的策略，具有\(\widetilde{\mathcal O}(ε^{-2})\)的样本保证，且无需访问数据生成分布。实验上，PDOCRL在标准离线约束RL基准测试中与强基线方法具有竞争力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses offline constrained reinforcement learning under partial data coverage, where prior methods often require full coverage or knowledge of the data-generating distribution. The authors propose PDOCRL, an oracle-efficient primal-dual algorithm that uses a decomposed linear-programming formulation to treat the policy as an explicit optimization variable, avoiding the need for policy extraction. Theoretically, under a stronger realizability condition and partial coverage of an optimal policy, PDOCRL achieves a near-optimal, near-feasible policy with a sample complexity of \(\widetilde{\mathcal O}(ε^{-2})\). Empirically, PDOCRL performs competitively against strong baselines on standard offline constrained RL benchmarks.
该论文研究了部分数据覆盖下的离线约束强化学习问题，现有方法通常需要完整数据覆盖或数据生成分布的知识。作者提出了PDOCRL，一种基于分解线性规划公式的原对偶算法，将策略作为显式优化变量，避免了策略提取步骤。理论上，在更强的可实现性条件和最优策略的部分覆盖下，PDOCRL能以\(\widetilde{\mathcal O}(ε^{-2})\)的样本复杂度返回近似最优且近似可行的策略。实验表明，PDOCRL在标准离线约束强化学习基准上表现与强基线方法相当。
Evolutionary Task Discovery: Advancing Reasoning Frontiers via Skill Composition and Complexity Scaling
Authors: Liqin Ye, Yanbin Yin, Michael Galarnyk, Yuzhao Heng, Sudheer Chava, Chao Zhang
First: 2026-05-12T07:26:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T07:26:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The reasoning frontier of Large Language Models (LLMs) has advanced significantly through modern post-training paradigms (e.g., Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR)). However, the efficacy of these methods remains fundamentally constrained by the diversity and complexity of the training data. One practical solution is data synthesis; yet, prevalent methods relying on unstructured mutation or exploration suffer from homogeneity collapse, failing to systematically expand the reasoning frontier. To overcome this, we propose Evoutionary Task Discovery (EvoTD), a framework that treats data synthesis as a directed search over a dual-axis manifold of Algorithmic Skills and Complexity Attributes. We introduce structured evolutionary operators to navigate this space: a Crossover operator that synthesizes novel skill compositions to enhance diversity, and a Parametric Mutation operator that scales structural constraints (e.g., input size, tree depth) to drive robust generalization. Crucially, we integrate a dynamic Zone of Proximal Development filter, ensuring tasks lie within the learnable region of the model. Empirically, EvoTD delivers substantial reasoning gains that generalize consistently across model architectures, pretraining regimes, and scales, demonstrating that structured evolutionary curricula can effectively support reasoning improvement. We release our code on https://github.com/liqinye/EvoTD.
中文标题/摘要
标题：进化式任务发现：通过技能组合与复杂度扩展推进推理前沿
大型语言模型（LLMs）的推理前沿已通过现代后训练范式（如基于可验证奖励的强化学习，RLVR）取得显著进展。然而，这些方法的有效性仍从根本上受限于训练数据的多样性和复杂度。一种实用解决方案是数据合成；但当前依赖非结构化变异或探索的主流方法易陷入同质性崩溃，无法系统性地拓展推理前沿。为此，我们提出进化式任务发现（EvoTD），该框架将数据合成视为在算法技能与复杂度属性双轴流形上的定向搜索。我们引入结构化进化算子以导航该空间：交叉算子通过合成新颖技能组合增强多样性，参数变异算子通过扩展结构约束（如输入规模、树深度）驱动鲁棒泛化。关键地，我们整合了动态最近发展区过滤器，确保任务位于模型可学习区域内。实验表明，EvoTD在多种模型架构、预训练范式及规模上持续带来显著的推理增益，证明结构化进化课程可有效支持推理能力提升。我们已在https://github.com/liqinye/EvoTD开源代码。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of current post-training methods for Large Language Models (LLMs), which are constrained by the diversity and complexity of training data, often leading to homogeneity collapse in data synthesis. To overcome this, the authors propose Evolutionary Task Discovery (EvoTD), a framework that treats data synthesis as a directed search over a dual-axis manifold of Algorithmic Skills and Complexity Attributes, using structured evolutionary operators: a Crossover operator for novel skill compositions and a Parametric Mutation operator for scaling structural constraints, integrated with a dynamic Zone of Proximal Development filter to ensure tasks are learnable. Experimental results show that EvoTD achieves substantial reasoning gains that generalize consistently across different model architectures, pretraining regimes, and scales, demonstrating the effectiveness of structured evolutionary curricula for reasoning improvement.

Priority-Driven Control and Communication in Decentralized Multi-Agent Systems via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Qingyun Guo, Junyi Shi, Tomasz Piotr Kucner, Dominik Baumann
First: 2026-05-11T12:43:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T07:11:47+00:00
Comments: Accepted to the 23rd IFAC World Congress
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Event-triggered control provides a mechanism for avoiding excessive use of constrained communication bandwidth in networked multi-agent systems. However, most existing methods rely on accurate system models, which may be unavailable in practice. In this work, we propose a model-free, priority-driven reinforcement learning algorithm that learns communication priorities and control policies jointly from data in decentralized multi-agent systems. By learning communication priorities, we circumvent the hybrid action space typical in event-triggered control with binary communication decisions. We evaluate our algorithm on benchmark tasks and demonstrate that it outperforms the baseline method.

Value-Decomposed Reinforcement Learning Framework for Taxiway Routing with Hierarchical Conflict-Aware Observations
Authors: Shizhong Zhou, Haifeng Liu, Zheng Zhang, Shiyu Zhang, Bo Yang, Yi Lin
First: 2026-05-09T07:32:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T07:08:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Taxiway routing and on-surface conflict avoidance are coupled safety-critical decision problems in airport surface operations. Existing planning and optimization methods are often limited by online computational cost, while reinforcement learning methods may struggle to represent downstream traffic conflicts and balance multiple objectives. This paper presents Conflict-aware Taxiway Routing (CaTR), a reinforcement learning framework for real-time multi-aircraft taxiway routing. CaTR constructs a grid-based airport surface environment with action masking, introduces a hierarchical foresight traffic representation to encode current and downstream conflict-related traffic conditions, and adopts a value-decomposed reinforcement learning strategy to prioritize sparse but safety-critical objectives. Experiments are conducted on a realistic environment based on Changsha Huanghua International Airport under multiple traffic density levels. Results show that CaTR achieves better safety--efficiency trade-offs than representative planning, optimization, and reinforcement learning baselines while maintaining practical runtime.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于价值分解的强化学习框架：面向层次化冲突感知的滑行道路径规划
滑行道路径规划与场面冲突避免是机场场面运行中相互耦合的安全关键决策问题。现有规划与优化方法常受限于在线计算成本，而强化学习方法则难以表征下游交通冲突并平衡多目标。本文提出冲突感知滑行道路径规划（CaTR），一种用于实时多航空器滑行道路径规划的强化学习框架。CaTR构建了基于网格的机场场面环境并采用动作掩码，引入层次化前瞻交通表征以编码当前及下游冲突相关交通状态，并采用价值分解强化学习策略优先处理稀疏但安全关键的目标。基于长沙黄花国际机场真实环境，在多种交通密度水平下开展实验。结果表明，CaTR在保持实用运行时间的同时，相比代表性规划、优化及强化学习基线方法实现了更优的安全-效率权衡。

The authors propose Conflict-aware Taxiway Routing (CaTR), a reinforcement learning framework that constructs a grid-based environment with action masking, introduces a hierarchical foresight traffic representation to encode current and downstream conflict-related conditions, and uses a value-decomposed strategy to prioritize sparse safety-critical objectives. Experiments on a realistic environment based on Changsha Huanghua International Airport under multiple traffic densities show that CaTR achieves better safety-efficiency trade-offs than representative baselines while maintaining practical runtime.

CuSearch: Curriculum Rollout Sampling via Search Depth for Agentic RAG
Authors: Jianghan Shen, Siqi Luo, Xinyu Cheng, Jing Xiong, Yue Li, Jiyao Liu, Jiashi Lin, Yirong Chen, Junjun He
First: 2026-05-12T06:42:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T06:42:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a promising paradigm for training agentic retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems from outcome-only supervision. Most existing methods optimize policies from uniformly sampled rollouts, implicitly treating all trajectories as equally informative. However, trajectories differ substantially in search depth and are therefore not equally informative: deeper-search trajectories contain more retrieval decision points and provide denser direct supervision for the retrieval sub-policy. Moreover, this heterogeneity grows over training as the within-batch depth distribution shifts toward higher values, yet uniform rollout sampling remains blind to this shift. To address this, we propose CuSearch, a curriculum rollout sampling framework built on Search-Depth Greedy Allocation (SDGA), a batch-level operator that reallocates a fixed update budget toward deeper-search trajectories. SDGA-Auto always targets the deepest available trajectories in the current batch, yielding an implicit training-aligned curriculum as the depth distribution shifts upward. SDGA-Phase explicitly advances the curriculum threshold as deeper trajectories become sufficiently abundant. Experiments across model types and retrieval frameworks show that CuSearch consistently improves performance, achieving up to 11.8 exact-match points over standard GRPO on ZeroSearch. These results establish per-trajectory search depth as a reliable, annotation-free proxy for retrieval supervision density in RLVR-based agentic RAG training. The code is available at https://github.com/MrToser/CuSearch.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CuSearch：基于搜索深度的课程式展开采样方法用于智能体检索增强生成
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为一种有前景的范式，用于仅从结果监督中训练智能体检索增强生成（RAG）系统。现有方法大多从均匀采样的展开轨迹中优化策略，隐含地将所有轨迹视为同等信息量。然而，不同轨迹在搜索深度上存在显著差异，因此信息量并不相同：深度搜索轨迹包含更多检索决策点，并为检索子策略提供更密集的直接监督。此外，这种异质性在训练过程中会加剧，因为批次内深度分布会向更高值偏移，而均匀展开采样对此偏移视而不见。为解决这一问题，我们提出CuSearch，一种基于搜索深度贪婪分配（SDGA）的课程式展开采样框架。SDGA是一种批次级算子，可将固定更新预算重新分配给更深搜索轨迹。SDGA-Auto始终针对当前批次中最深的可用轨迹，随着深度分布上移，形成隐式的训练对齐课程。SDGA-Phase则在更深轨迹足够丰富时显式推进课程阈值。跨模型类型和检索框架的实验表明，CuSearch能持续提升性能，在ZeroSearch上相比标准GRPO最高提升11.8个精确匹配点。这些结果确立了每条轨迹的搜索深度作为RLVR智能体RAG训练中检索监督密度的可靠、免标注代理指标。代码已开源：https://github.com/MrToser/CuSearch。
Summary / 总结
CuSearch addresses the limitation of uniform rollout sampling in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards for agentic retrieval-augmented generation, where trajectories with deeper search provide denser supervision for the retrieval sub-policy. The method introduces a curriculum rollout sampling framework based on Search-Depth Greedy Allocation, which reallocates the update budget toward deeper-search trajectories, with two variants: SDGA-Auto for implicit training-aligned curriculum and SDGA-Phase for explicit threshold advancement. Experiments across model types and retrieval frameworks show consistent performance improvements, achieving up to 11.8 exact-match points over standard GRPO on ZeroSearch, establishing search depth as a reliable proxy for supervision density.
CuSearch针对基于可验证奖励的强化学习在智能检索增强生成中的均匀轨迹采样问题，提出深度搜索轨迹能提供更密集的检索子策略监督信号。该方法基于搜索深度贪婪分配构建课程式轨迹采样框架，通过将更新预算重新分配给更深搜索轨迹，包含隐式课程对齐的SDGA-Auto和显式阈值推进的SDGA-Phase两种变体。跨模型类型和检索框架的实验表明，该方法在ZeroSearch上相比标准GRPO最多提升11.8个精确匹配点，验证了搜索深度可作为监督密度的可靠代理指标。
Sparse Offline Reinforcement Learning with Corruption Robustness
Authors: Nam Phuong Tran, Andi Nika, Goran Radanovic, Long Tran-Thanh, Debmalya Mandal
First: 2025-12-31T10:28:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T06:35:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We investigate robustness to strong data corruption in offline sparse reinforcement learning (RL). In our setting, an adversary may arbitrarily perturb a fraction of the collected trajectories from a high-dimensional but sparse Markov decision process, and our goal is to estimate a near optimal policy. The main challenge is that, in the high-dimensional regime where the number of samples $N$ is smaller than the feature dimension $d$, exploiting sparsity is essential for obtaining non-vacuous guarantees but has not been systematically studied in offline RL. We analyse the problem under uniform coverage and sparse single-concentrability assumptions. While Least Square Value Iteration (LSVI), a standard approach for robust offline RL, performs well under uniform coverage, we show that integrating sparsity into LSVI is unnatural, and its analysis may break down due to overly pessimistic bonuses. To overcome this, we propose actor-critic methods with sparse robust estimator oracles, which avoid the use of pointwise pessimistic bonuses and provide the first non-vacuous guarantees for sparse offline RL under single-policy concentrability coverage. Moreover, we extend our results to the contaminated setting and show that our algorithm remains robust under strong contamination. Our results provide the first non-vacuous guarantees in high-dimensional sparse MDPs with single-policy concentrability coverage and corruption, showing that learning a near-optimal policy remains possible in regimes where traditional robust offline RL techniques may fail.
中文标题/摘要
标题：具有鲁棒性的稀疏离线强化学习
我们研究了离线稀疏强化学习中对强数据损坏的鲁棒性。在我们的设定中，对手可能任意扰动从高维但稀疏的马尔可夫决策过程中收集的轨迹的一部分，我们的目标是估计一个接近最优的策略。主要挑战在于，在高维场景下（样本数量N小于特征维度d），利用稀疏性对于获得非平凡保证至关重要，但在离线强化学习中尚未得到系统研究。我们在均匀覆盖和稀疏单可集中性假设下分析了该问题。虽然最小二乘值迭代（LSVI）作为标准鲁棒离线强化学习方法在均匀覆盖下表现良好，但我们表明将稀疏性整合到LSVI中并不自然，且其分析可能因过于悲观的奖励而失效。为解决此问题，我们提出了带有稀疏鲁棒估计器或acles的演员-评论家方法，避免了逐点悲观奖励的使用，并在单策略可集中性覆盖下首次为稀疏离线强化学习提供了非平凡保证。此外，我们将结果扩展到污染场景，并表明我们的算法在强污染下仍保持鲁棒性。我们的结果首次在高维稀疏MDP中提供了具有单策略可集中性覆盖和损坏的非平凡保证，表明在传统鲁棒离线强化学习技术可能失效的场景下，学习接近最优策略仍然是可能的。

本文研究在强数据破坏下的高维稀疏离线强化学习问题，其中对手可任意扰动部分轨迹。作者发现标准方法如最小二乘值迭代（LSVI）因过于悲观的奖励而难以利用稀疏性，在单策略集中性覆盖下无法提供非平凡保证。为此，他们提出基于稀疏鲁棒估计器的演员-评论家方法，避免使用逐点悲观奖励，首次在单策略集中性覆盖和破坏下为稀疏离线RL提供非平凡保证。实验表明，该算法在传统鲁棒离线RL技术失效时仍能保持鲁棒性并学习近最优策略。
OUI as a Structural Observable: Towards an Activation-Centric View of Neural Network Training
Authors: Alberto Fernández-Hernández, Jose I. Mestre, Cristian Pérez-Corral, Manuel F. Dolz, Jose Duato, Enrique S. Quintana-Ortí
First: 2026-05-12T05:59:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T05:59:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Activation functions are what make deep networks expressive: without them, the model collapses to a linear map. Yet we still evaluate training mostly from the outside, through loss, accuracy, return, or final calibration, while the internal structural evolution of the network remains largely unobserved. In this paper, we argue that the Overfitting--Underfitting Indicator (OUI) should be understood as a first practical observable of that internal structure. Across our recent results, OUI consistently appears as an early, label-free, activation-based signal that reveals whether a network is entering a poor or promising training regime before convergence. In supervised learning, it anticipates weight decay regimes; in reinforcement learning, it discriminates learning-rate regimes early in PPO actor--critic; and in online control, it can drive layer-wise weight decay adaptation. Read together with recent evidence that activation patterns tend to stabilize earlier than parameters, these results suggest a broader research direction: an activation-centric theory of training dynamics. OUI is becoming an empirical foothold toward this theory.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OUI作为结构性可观测量：迈向以激活为中心的神经网络训练视角

BenchCAD: A Comprehensive, Industry-Standard Benchmark for Programmatic CAD
Authors: Haozhe Zhang, Kaichen Liu, Miaomiao Chen, Lei Li, Shaojie Yang, Cheng Peng, Hanjie Chen
First: 2026-05-11T17:13:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T05:46:14+00:00
Comments: 9 page 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Industrial Computer-Aided Design (CAD) code generation requires models to produce executable parametric programs from visual or textual inputs. Beyond recognizing the outer shape of a part, this task involves understanding its 3D structure, inferring engineering parameters, and choosing CAD operations that reflect how the part would be designed and manufactured. Despite the promise of Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) for this task, they are rarely evaluated on whether these capabilities jointly hold in realistic industrial CAD settings. We present BenchCAD, a unified benchmark for industrial CAD reasoning. BenchCAD contains 17,900 execution-verified CadQuery programs across 106 industrial part families, including bevel gears, compression springs, twist drills, and other reusable engineering designs. It evaluates models through visual question answering, code question answering, image-to-code generation, and instruction-guided code editing, enabling fine-grained analysis across perception, parametric abstraction, and executable program synthesis. Across 10+ frontier models, BenchCAD shows that current systems often recover coarse outer geometry but fail to produce faithful parametric CAD programs. Common failures include missing fine 3D structure, misinterpreting industrial design parameters, and replacing essential operations such as sweeps, lofts, and twist-extrudes with simpler sketch-and-extrude patterns. Fine-tuning and reinforcement learning improve in-distribution performance, but generalization to unseen part families remains limited. These results position BenchCAD as a benchmark for measuring and improving the industrial readiness of multimodal CAD automation.

Conflict-Aware Fusion: Mitigating Logic Inertia in Large Language Models via Structured Cognitive Priors
Authors: Qiming Bao, Xiaoxuan Fu, Michael Witbrock
First: 2025-12-06T10:49:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T04:53:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) achieve high accuracy on many reasoning benchmarks but remain brittle under structural perturbations of rule-based systems. We introduce a diagnostic framework with four stress tests -- redundant vs. essential rule deletion, contradictory-rule injection, logic-preserving rewrites, and multi-law stacking -- and use it to expose Logic Inertia: the tendency of generative LLMs (Qwen2/3, TinyLlama, GPT-4o, Gemma-3-4B-IT) and the encoder-only BERT baseline to persist along learned deductive trajectories under inconsistent premises. The collapse is sharp: untreated baselines fall from accuracy 1.00 on the base task to 0.00 on contradiction injection (instance-level exact match), and GPT-4o resolves only 56.0% of contradiction cases. We propose Conflict-Aware Fusion, a four-stage training pipeline that enforces verification-before-deduction as a learned structural prior: (i) SFT establishes the verification preamble; (ii) DPO sharpens the halt-on-contradiction decision boundary; (iii) Logical Invariance REgularisation (LIRE) penalises divergence between logically equivalent rule formulations via symmetric KL; (iv) Reinforcement Learning from Verification Feedback (RLVF) uses a symbolic forward-chaining engine as a deterministic oracle reward, jointly optimising invariance and sensitivity. The pipeline saturates all four primary stress tests for both 1.5B and 8B backbones. We further validate a Phase 2 extension that replaces the propositional oracle with a Lean 4 kernel, attaining 99.0% kernel agreement on the 105 classically-derivable (T) questions within a stratified 187-question Lean-translated sample (overall 71.7% across both polarities), providing a sound upgrade path to formally verified RL training. Code and benchmark: https://github.com/14H034160212/lemo
中文标题/摘要
标题：冲突感知融合：通过结构化认知先验缓解大语言模型中的逻辑惯性
大语言模型（LLMs）在许多推理基准上取得了高准确率，但在基于规则的系统的结构扰动下仍然脆弱。我们引入了一个包含四项压力测试的诊断框架——冗余与必要规则删除、矛盾规则注入、逻辑保持重写以及多定律叠加——并用其揭示了逻辑惯性：生成式LLMs（Qwen2/3、TinyLlama、GPT-4o、Gemma-3-4B-IT）以及仅编码器的BERT基线在矛盾前提条件下倾向于沿习得的演绎轨迹持续运行。这种崩溃是剧烈的：未经处理的基线在基础任务上准确率为1.00，在矛盾注入（实例级精确匹配）时降至0.00，而GPT-4o仅解决了56.0%的矛盾案例。我们提出了冲突感知融合，这是一个四阶段训练流程，将验证-前置于-演绎作为习得的结构化先验加以强化：（i）SFT建立验证前导；（ii）DPO锐化矛盾时停止的决策边界；（iii）逻辑不变正则化（LIRE）通过对称KL散度惩罚逻辑等价规则表述之间的差异；（iv）基于验证反馈的强化学习（RLVF）使用符号前向链接引擎作为确定性预言奖励，联合优化不变性与敏感性。该流程在1.5B和8B骨干网络上均饱和了所有四项主要压力测试。我们进一步验证了第二阶段扩展，将命题预言替换为Lean 4内核，在分层抽样的187个Lean翻译问题样本中，对105个经典可推导（T）问题达到了99.0%的内核一致性（整体跨两种极性为71.7%），为形式化验证的RL训练提供了可靠的升级路径。代码和基准：https://github.com/14H034160212/lemo
Summary / 总结
The paper identifies Logic Inertia in large language models, where models like Qwen2/3, TinyLlama, GPT-4o, and BERT persist along learned deductive trajectories under inconsistent premises, causing accuracy to drop from 1.00 to 0.00 on contradiction injection tasks. To address this, the authors propose Conflict-Aware Fusion, a four-stage training pipeline that enforces verification-before-deduction as a structural prior, combining supervised fine-tuning, direct preference optimization, logical invariance regularization via symmetric KL divergence, and reinforcement learning from verification feedback using a symbolic forward-chaining oracle. The method saturates all four primary stress tests for both 1.5B and 8B backbones, and a Phase 2 extension with a Lean 4 kernel achieves 99.0% kernel agreement on classically-derivable questions, demonstrating a sound path to formally verified reinforcement learning training.
该论文揭示了大型语言模型中的逻辑惯性现象，即Qwen2/3、TinyLlama、GPT-4o和BERT等模型在不一致前提条件下会沿习得的演绎轨迹持续推理，导致矛盾注入任务中准确率从1.00骤降至0.00。为解决此问题，作者提出冲突感知融合方法，这是一个四阶段训练流程，通过将验证前置演绎作为结构化先验，结合监督微调、直接偏好优化、基于对称KL散度的逻辑不变性正则化，以及利用符号前向链引擎作为确定性奖励的验证反馈强化学习。该方法在1.5B和8B骨干模型上通过了所有四项主要压力测试，且第二阶段扩展使用Lean 4内核在经典可推导问题上达到99.0%的内核一致性，为形式化验证的强化学习训练提供了可靠升级路径。
STAPO: Stabilizing Reinforcement Learning for LLMs by Silencing Rare Spurious Tokens
Authors: Shiqi Liu, Zeyu He, Guojian Zhan, Letian Tao, Zhilong Zheng, Jiang Wu, Yinuo Wang, Yang Guan, Kehua Sheng, Bo Zhang, Keqiang Li, Jingliang Duan, Shengbo Eben Li
First: 2026-02-17T14:46:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T04:42:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has significantly improved large language model reasoning, but existing RL fine-tuning methods rely heavily on heuristic techniques such as entropy regularization and reweighting to maintain stability. In practice, they often suffer from late-stage performance collapse, leading to degraded reasoning quality and unstable training. We identify a key factor behind this instability: a small fraction of tokens, termed spurious tokens (around 0.01%), which contribute little to the reasoning outcome but receive disproportionately amplified gradient updates due to inheriting the full sequence-level reward. We present a unified framework for evaluating token-level optimization impacts across spurious risk, gradient norms, and entropy changes. Building on the analysis of token characteristics that severely disrupt optimization, we propose the Silencing Spurious Tokens (S2T) mechanism to efficiently suppress their gradient perturbations. Incorporating this mechanism into a group-based objective, we propose Spurious-Token-Aware Policy Optimization (STAPO), which promotes stable and effective large-scale model refinement. Across six mathematical reasoning benchmarks using Qwen 1.7B, 8B, and 14B base models, STAPO consistently demonstrates superior entropy stability and achieves an average performance improvement of 11.49% ($ρ_{\mathrm{T}}$=1.0, top-p=1.0) and 3.73% ($ρ_{\mathrm{T}}$=0.7, top-p=0.9) over GRPO, 20-Entropy, and JustRL.
Summary / 总结
The paper identifies that instability in reinforcement learning fine-tuning for large language models, often leading to performance collapse, is caused by a tiny fraction of tokens (about 0.01%) called spurious tokens, which receive disproportionately large gradient updates from inheriting full sequence-level rewards despite contributing little to reasoning outcomes. To address this, the authors propose a unified framework to evaluate token-level optimization impacts and introduce the Silencing Spurious Tokens (S2T) mechanism to suppress these gradient perturbations, integrated into a group-based objective called Spurious-Token-Aware Policy Optimization (STAPO). Experiments on six mathematical reasoning benchmarks using Qwen 1.7B, 8B, and 14B models show that STAPO consistently achieves superior entropy stability and outperforms GRPO, 20-Entropy, and JustRL, with average performance improvements of 11.49% and 3.73% under different settings.
该论文发现，在大型语言模型的强化学习微调中，导致性能崩溃的不稳定性主要由一小部分（约0.01%）称为虚假令牌的令牌引起，这些令牌虽然对推理结果贡献甚微，但因继承完整的序列级奖励而获得不成比例的大梯度更新。为解决此问题，作者提出了一个统一框架来评估令牌级优化影响，并引入了一种沉默虚假令牌机制来抑制其梯度扰动，将其整合到基于组的目标函数中，形成虚假令牌感知策略优化。在Qwen 1.7B、8B和14B模型上的六个数学推理基准测试中，STAPO始终展现出优越的熵稳定性，并在不同设置下平均性能比GRPO、20-Entropy和JustRL分别提升11.49%和3.73%。
Post-ADC Inference: Valid Inference After Active Data Collection
Authors: Shuichi Nishino, Tomohiro Shiraishi, Teruyuki Katsuoka, Ichiro Takeuchi
First: 2026-05-12T04:27:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T04:27:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The validity of statistical inference depends critically on how data are collected. When data gathered through active data collection (ADC) are reused for a post-hoc inferential task, conventional inference can fail because the sampling is adaptively biased toward regions favored by the collection strategy. This issue is especially pronounced in black-box optimization, where sequential model-based optimization (SMBO) methods such as the tree-structured Parzen estimator (TPE) and Gaussian process upper confidence bound (GP-UCB) preferentially concentrate evaluations in promising regions. We study statistical inference on actively collected data when the inferential target is constructed in a data-dependent manner after data collection. To enable valid inference in this setting, we propose post-ADC inference, a framework that accounts for the biases arising from both the active data collection process and the subsequent data-driven target construction. Our method builds on selective inference and provides valid $p$-values and confidence intervals that correct for both sources of bias. The framework applies to a broad class of ADC processes by imposing only assumptions on the observation noise, without requiring any assumptions on the underlying black-box function or the surrogate model used by the SMBO algorithm. Empirical results also show that post-ADC inference provides valid inference for data collected by GP-UCB and TPE.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the failure of conventional statistical inference when data collected through active data collection (ADC) methods, such as sequential model-based optimization (SMBO) like TPE and GP-UCB, are reused for post-hoc inferential tasks, due to adaptive sampling biases. The authors propose a post-ADC inference framework based on selective inference that corrects for biases from both the active data collection process and data-dependent target construction, requiring only assumptions on observation noise. Empirical results demonstrate that the method provides valid p-values and confidence intervals for data collected by GP-UCB and TPE.
该论文探讨了当通过主动数据收集方法（如TPE和GP-UCB等序列模型优化方法）收集的数据被用于事后推断任务时，由于自适应采样偏差导致传统统计推断失效的问题。作者提出了一种基于选择性推断的后ADC推断框架，该框架能校正来自主动数据收集过程和后续数据驱动目标构建的双重偏差，仅需对观测噪声做出假设。实验结果表明，该方法能为GP-UCB和TPE收集的数据提供有效的p值和置信区间。
Hierarchical LLM-Driven Control for HAPS-Assisted UAV Networks: Joint Optimization of Flight and Connectivity
Authors: Zijiang Yan, Hao Zhou, Wael Jaafar, Jianhua Pei, Ping Wang, Halim Yanikomeroglu, Hina Tabassum
First: 2026-05-12T04:27:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T04:27:14+00:00
Comments: Submission for possible publication
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Uncrewed aerial vehicles (UAVs) are increasingly deployed in complex networked environments, yet the joint optimization of multi-UAV motion control and connectivity remains a fundamental challenge. In this paper, we study a multi-UAV system operating in an integrated terrestrial and non-terrestrial network (ITNTN) comprising terrestrial base stations and high-altitude platform stations (HAPS). We consider a three-dimensional (3D) aerial highway scenario where UAVs must adapt their motion to ensure collision avoidance, efficient traffic flow, and reliable communication under dynamic and partially observable conditions. We first model the problem as a hierarchical multi-objective partially observable Markov decision process (H-MO-POMDP), capturing the coupling between control and communication objectives. Based on this formulation, we propose a large language model (LLM)-driven hierarchical multi-rate control framework. At the global level, an LLM-based controller on the HAPS performs long-term planning for load balancing and handover decisions. At the local level, each UAV employs a hybrid controller that integrates a slow-timescale LLM for high-level spatial reasoning with a reinforcement learning agent for faster UAV-to-infrastructure (U2I) communication and motion control. We further develop a high-fidelity 3D simulation platform by integrating the gym-pybullet-drones environment with 3GPP-compliant RF/THz channel models. Numerical results demonstrate that the proposed framework significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving a 14% increase in transportation efficiency and a 25% improvement in telecommunication throughput. Additionally, it achieves a 23% reduction in physical collision rates, demonstrating strong handover stability and zero-shot generalization in dynamic scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于分层大语言模型驱动的HAPS辅助无人机网络控制：飞行与连接联合优化
无人机（UAV）越来越多地部署在复杂的网络化环境中，但多无人机运动控制与连接的联合优化仍是一项基本挑战。本文研究了一个在集成地面与非地面网络（ITNTN）中运行的多无人机系统，该系统包含地面基站和高空平台站（HAPS）。我们考虑了一个三维（3D）空中高速公路场景，其中无人机必须调整其运动，以确保在动态和部分可观测条件下的碰撞避免、高效交通流和可靠通信。我们首先将问题建模为分层多目标部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（H-MO-POMDP），捕捉控制与通信目标之间的耦合。基于此公式，我们提出了一种大语言模型（LLM）驱动的分层多速率控制框架。在全局层面，HAPS上的基于LLM的控制器执行长期规划，用于负载均衡和切换决策。在局部层面，每架无人机采用混合控制器，将慢时间尺度的LLM用于高级空间推理，与强化学习代理用于更快的无人机到基础设施（U2I）通信和运动控制相结合。我们进一步通过将gym-pybullet-drones环境与符合3GPP标准的射频/太赫兹信道模型集成，开发了一个高保真3D仿真平台。数值结果表明，所提出的框架显著优于最先进的基线，实现了运输效率提高14%和电信吞吐量提高25%。此外，物理碰撞率降低了23%，在动态场景中表现出强大的切换稳定性和零样本泛化能力。

This paper addresses the joint optimization of motion control and connectivity in multi-UAV systems operating within integrated terrestrial and non-terrestrial networks (ITNTN) featuring HAPS. The authors model the problem as a hierarchical multi-objective POMDP and propose an LLM-driven hierarchical multi-rate control framework, where a global LLM on the HAPS handles long-term planning while local UAVs combine a slow-timescale LLM for spatial reasoning with a reinforcement learning agent for fast communication and motion control. Selective Off-Policy Reference Tuning with Plan Guidance
Authors: Duc Anh Le, Tien-Phat Nguyen, Thien Huu Nguyen, Linh Ngo Van, Trung Le
First: 2026-05-12T04:25:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T04:25:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards helps reasoning, but GRPO-style methods stall on hard prompts where all sampled rollouts fail. SORT adds a repair update for those failures without changing rollout generation: it derives a plan from the reference solution, compares token probabilities with and without that plan, and gives higher weight to tokens that become more predictable under plan conditioning. This turns all-wrong prompts into selective, structure-aware learning signals instead of uniform imitation. Across three backbones and eight reasoning benchmarks, SORT improves over GRPO and guidance baselines, with largest gains on weaker models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于计划引导的选择性离策略参考调优
基于可验证奖励的强化学习有助于推理，但GRPO类方法在困难提示上会停滞，因为所有采样轨迹均失败。SORT针对这些失败添加了修复更新，而不改变轨迹生成方式：它从参考解中推导出计划，比较有无该计划下的词元概率，并对在计划条件下变得更可预测的词元赋予更高权重。这将全错提示转化为选择性、结构感知的学习信号，而非统一模仿。在三个骨干模型和八个推理基准上，SORT相比GRPO及引导基线均有提升，且在较弱模型上增益最大。

The paper proposes Selective Off-Policy Reference Tuning (SORT) to address the limitation of GRPO-style reinforcement learning methods that stall on hard prompts where all sampled rollouts fail. SORT introduces a repair update that derives a plan from the reference solution, compares token probabilities with and without that plan, and assigns higher weight to tokens that become more predictable under plan conditioning, thereby converting all-wrong prompts into selective, structure-aware learning signals. Experimental results across three backbones and eight reasoning benchmarks show that SORT consistently outperforms GRPO and guidance baselines, with the largest gains observed on weaker models.
该论文提出选择性离策略参考调优（SORT）方法，以解决GRPO风格强化学习方法在困难提示上所有采样轨迹均失败时停滞不前的问题。SORT通过从参考解中推导计划，比较有无计划条件下的令牌概率，并对在计划条件下更可预测的令牌赋予更高权重，从而将全错提示转化为选择性、结构感知的学习信号。在三个骨干网络和八个推理基准上的实验结果表明，SORT始终优于GRPO和引导基线方法，且在较弱模型上提升最为显著。
Understanding and Preventing Entropy Collapse in RLVR with On-Policy Entropy Flow Optimization
Authors: Huimin Xu, Shuai Zhao, Xiaobao Wu, Anh Tuan Luu
First: 2026-05-12T04:08:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T04:08:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has become an effective paradigm for improving the reasoning ability of large language models. However, widely used RLVR algorithms, such as GRPO, often suffer from entropy collapse, leading to premature determinism and unstable optimization. Existing remedies, including entropy regularization and ratio-based clipping heuristics, either control entropy in a coarse-grained manner or rely on approximate on-policy training. In this paper, we revisit entropy collapse from a token-level entropy flow perspective. Our analysis reveals that entropy-decreasing tokens consistently outweigh entropy-increasing ones, resulting in a severely imbalanced entropy flow. This perspective provides a unified explanation of entropy collapse in existing RLVR algorithms and highlights the importance of balancing entropy dynamics. Motivated by this analysis, we propose On-Policy Entropy Flow Optimization (OPEFO), an adaptive entropy flow balancing mechanism that rescales entropy-increasing and entropy-decreasing updates according to their contributions to entropy change, while remaining strict on-policy. Experiments on six mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that OPEFO improves training stability and final performance. We will release the code and models upon publication.
中文标题/摘要
标题：理解与预防基于可验证奖励的强化学习中的熵坍塌：基于同策略熵流优化的方法
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为提升大语言模型推理能力的有效范式。然而，广泛使用的RLVR算法（如GRPO）常遭遇熵坍塌问题，导致过早确定性和不稳定优化。现有补救措施（包括熵正则化和基于比率的裁剪启发式方法）要么以粗粒度方式控制熵，要么依赖近似的同策略训练。本文从词元级熵流视角重新审视熵坍塌。我们的分析揭示，熵减词元持续超过熵增词元，导致严重失衡的熵流。这一视角为现有RLVR算法中的熵坍塌提供了统一解释，并凸显了平衡熵动态的重要性。基于此分析，我们提出同策略熵流优化（OPEFO），这是一种自适应熵流平衡机制，根据熵增和熵减更新对熵变化的贡献重新缩放它们，同时保持严格同策略。在六个数学推理基准上的实验表明，OPEFO提升了训练稳定性和最终性能。我们将在论文发表后发布代码和模型。
