The paper addresses entropy collapse in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for large language models, where algorithms like GRPO suffer from premature determinism and unstable optimization. The authors analyze this issue from a token-level entropy flow perspective, finding that entropy-decreasing tokens consistently outnumber entropy-increasing ones, leading to imbalanced entropy dynamics. They propose On-Policy Entropy Flow Optimization (OPEFO), an adaptive mechanism that rescales updates based on their contribution to entropy change while maintaining strict on-policy training. Experiments on six mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that OPEFO improves training stability and final performance.
该论文针对强化学习与可验证奖励（RLVR）中大语言模型出现的熵崩溃问题，即GRPO等算法因过早确定性导致优化不稳定。作者从词元级熵流角度分析，发现熵减少词元始终多于熵增加词元，造成熵动态严重失衡。为此提出在线策略熵流优化（OPEFO），一种根据熵变化贡献自适应缩放更新并保持严格在线策略的机制。在六个数学推理基准上的实验表明，OPEFO提升了训练稳定性和最终性能。
An End-to-End Framework for Building Large Language Models for Software Operations
Authors: Jingkai He, Pengfei Chen, Chenghui Wu, Shuang Liang, Ye Li, Gou Tan, Xiadao Wen, Chuanfu Zhang
First: 2026-04-06T02:40:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T03:51:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In the field of software operations, Large Language Models (LLMs) have attracted increasing attention. However, existing research has not yet achieved efficient and effective end-to-end intelligent operations due to low-quality data, fragmented knowledge and insufficient learning. To explore the potential of LLMs in software operations, we propose OpsLLM, a domain-specific LLM that supports both knowledge-based question answering (QA) and root cause analysis (RCA). Moreover, we disclose the detailed workflow for building LLMs specifically in the software operations domain. First, a Human-in-the-Loop mechanism is introduced to curate highquality data from a large collection of operational raw data and construct a fine-tuning dataset. Then, based on the data, supervised fine-tuning is conducted to achieve a base model. Furthermore, we introduce a domain process reward model (DPRM) during the reinforcement learning stage to optimize the accuracy and reliability of the fine-tuned model on RCA tasks. Experimental results on the tasks with diverse difficulties demonstrate that OpsLLMs effectively learns and aligns with the operational domain knowledge infused, outperforming existing open-source and closed-source LLMs in accuracy with improvements of 0.2%~5.7% on QA tasks and 2.7% ~70.3% on RCA tasks, while exhibiting strong transferability. Moreover, we will open-source three versions of OpsLLM with 7B, 14B and 32B parameters, along with a 15K fine-tuning dataset.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向软件运维的大型语言模型端到端构建框架
在软件运维领域，大型语言模型（LLM）日益受到关注。然而，现有研究因数据质量低、知识碎片化及学习不充分，尚未实现高效且有效的端到端智能运维。为探索LLM在软件运维中的潜力，我们提出OpsLLM——一种支持基于知识的问答（QA）和根因分析（RCA）的领域专用LLM。此外，我们公开了在软件运维领域构建LLM的详细工作流程。首先，引入人在回路机制，从大量运维原始数据中筛选高质量数据，构建微调数据集。然后，基于该数据进行监督微调以获得基础模型。进一步，在强化学习阶段引入领域过程奖励模型（DPRM），以优化微调模型在RCA任务上的准确性和可靠性。在多种难度任务上的实验结果表明，OpsLLM能有效学习并融合注入的运维领域知识，在QA任务上准确率提升0.2%~5.7%，在RCA任务上提升2.7%~70.3%，优于现有开源和闭源LLM，并展现出强迁移性。此外，我们将开源三个版本的OpsLLM（7B、14B和32B参数）及一个15K微调数据集。

TOPPO: Rethinking PPO for Multi-Task Reinforcement Learning with Critic Balancing
Authors: Yuanpeng Li, Gefei Lin, Annie Qu, Rui Miao
First: 2026-05-12T03:40:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T03:40:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) and its variants dominate Multi-Task Reinforcement Learning (MTRL) due to their off-policy sample efficiency, while on-policy methods such as Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) remain underexplored. We diagnose that PPO in MTRL suffers from a previously overlooked issue: critic-side gradient ill-conditioning, which may cause tail tasks to stall while easy tasks dominate the value function's updates. To address this, we propose TOPPO (Tail-Optimized PPO), a reformulation of PPO via Critic Balancing -- a set of modules that improve gradient conditioning and balance learning dynamics across tasks. Unlike prior approaches that rely on modular architectures or large models, TOPPO targets the optimization bottleneck within PPO itself. Empirically, TOPPO achieves stronger mean and tail-task performance than published SAC-family and ARS-family baselines while using substantially fewer parameters and environment steps on Meta-World+ benchmark. Notably, TOPPO matches or surpasses strong SAC baselines early in training and maintains superior performance at full budget. Ablations confirm the effectiveness of each module in TOPPO and provide insights into their interactions. Our results demonstrate that, with proper optimization, on-policy methods can rival or exceed off-policy approaches in MTRL, challenging the prevailing reliance on SAC and highlighting critic-side gradient conditioning as the central bottleneck.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TOPPO：通过评论家平衡重新思考多任务强化学习中的PPO
软演员-评论家（SAC）及其变体由于离策略的样本效率在多任务强化学习（MTRL）中占据主导地位，而近端策略优化（PPO）等在线策略方法仍未得到充分探索。我们发现PPO在MTRL中存在一个先前被忽视的问题：评论家端的梯度病态，这可能导致尾部任务停滞，而简单任务主导价值函数的更新。为解决此问题，我们提出TOPPO（尾部优化PPO），通过评论家平衡（一组改善梯度条件并平衡跨任务学习动态的模块）重新构建PPO。与依赖模块化架构或大型模型的先前方法不同，TOPPO针对PPO自身的优化瓶颈。实验表明，TOPPO在Meta-World+基准上使用显著更少的参数和环境步数，实现了比已发表的SAC系列和ARS系列基线更强的平均和尾部任务性能。值得注意的是，TOPPO在训练早期就匹配或超越强SAC基线，并在完整预算下保持优越性能。消融实验证实了TOPPO中每个模块的有效性，并提供了对其交互作用的见解。我们的结果表明，通过适当优化，在线策略方法可以在MTRL中与离策略方法相媲美或超越，挑战了当前对SAC的依赖，并突显了评论家端梯度条件作为核心瓶颈。
Summary / 总结
The paper identifies that Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) underperforms in multi-task reinforcement learning due to a previously overlooked critic-side gradient ill-conditioning problem, where easy tasks dominate value function updates and cause tail tasks to stall. To address this, the authors propose TOPPO (Tail-Optimized PPO), which reformulates PPO through Critic Balancing—a set of modules that improve gradient conditioning and balance learning dynamics across tasks without relying on modular architectures or large models. Empirically, TOPPO achieves stronger mean and tail-task performance than published SAC-family and ARS-family baselines on Meta-World+ benchmark while using substantially fewer parameters and environment steps, matching or surpassing strong SAC baselines early in training and maintaining superior performance at full budget.
该论文发现PPO在多任务强化学习中表现不佳，是因为一个此前被忽视的问题：评论家端的梯度病态，导致简单任务主导价值函数更新，而困难任务停滞不前。为此，作者提出TOPPO，通过评论家平衡模块集重新设计PPO，改善梯度条件并平衡各任务的学习动态，无需依赖模块化架构或大模型。实验表明，在Meta-World+基准上，TOPPO以更少的参数和环境交互步数，在平均性能和尾部任务性能上均超越已发表的SAC系列和ARS系列基线，在训练早期就能匹敌或超越强SAC基线，并在完整预算下保持更优性能。
Robust Multi-Agent Path Finding under Observation Attacks: A Principled Adversarial-Plus-Smoothing Training Recipe
Authors: Riad Ahmed
First: 2026-05-12T03:33:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T03:33:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Decentralized multi-agent path finding (MAPF) routes a team of agents on a shared grid, each acting from its own local view. The standard solution trains one shared neural policy with Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO), a popular on-policy reinforcement learning algorithm. Such a policy works well on clean observations, but a small input perturbation on one agent often changes its action, which then blocks a neighbour, and the team jams. In this paper we present two training recipes that keep the same network and the same deployment loop, yet make the policy hold up under perturbed observations. The first recipe, Adv-PPO, trains the shared policy against worst-case perturbations of its own input and selects the checkpoint by performance under adversarial perturbation. The second recipe, Adv-PPO+MACER, fine-tunes that checkpoint with a small on-policy smoothness term whose gradient follows the certified radius of randomized smoothing. On POGEMA with 8x8 maps and four agents, the unprotected PPO policy reaches 95.8% clean success but only 2.5% under the strongest attack. Adv-PPO recovers worst-case success to 59.2% at one percentage point of clean cost. Adv-PPO+MACER recovers it to 77.5% +/- 6.0% across three independent seeds at less than one percentage point of clean cost. We support these numbers with per-attack curves, a certified action-stability sanity check (which measures the smoothed-policy wrapper, not the deployed argmax policy), and side-by-side rollout storyboards that show the failure mode and the fix inside one environment instance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：观测攻击下鲁棒的多智能体路径规划：一种原则性的对抗加平滑训练方案
分散式多智能体路径规划（MAPF）在共享网格上为智能体团队规划路径，每个智能体基于自身局部视角行动。标准方案使用近端策略优化（PPO）这一流行的在线策略强化学习算法训练共享神经策略。该策略在干净观测下表现良好，但单个智能体的微小输入扰动常导致其动作改变，进而阻塞邻居，造成团队拥堵。本文提出两种训练方案，保持相同网络与部署流程，却使策略在扰动观测下保持鲁棒。第一种方案Adv-PPO，针对自身输入的最坏情况扰动训练共享策略，并根据对抗扰动下的性能选择检查点。第二种方案Adv-PPO+MACER，通过小规模在线策略平滑项微调该检查点，其梯度遵循随机平滑的认证半径。在8x8地图与四个智能体的POGEMA环境中，未受保护的PPO策略在干净环境下成功率达95.8%，但在最强攻击下仅2.5%。Adv-PPO以1%的干净性能代价将最坏情况成功率恢复至59.2%。Adv-PPO+MACER以不到1%的干净性能代价，在三个独立随机种子下将成功率恢复至77.5%±6.0%。我们通过逐攻击曲线、认证动作稳定性合理性检查（衡量平滑策略包装器，而非部署的argmax策略）以及并排展开故事板（展示单个环境实例中的故障模式与修复）来支撑这些数据。

On 8x8 POGEMA maps with four agents, the unprotected PPO policy achieves 95.8% clean success but only 2.5% under the strongest attack, while Adv-PPO recovers worst-case success to 59.2% with a 1% clean cost penalty, and Adv-PPO+MACER further improves it to 77.5% ± 6.0% across three seeds with less than 1% clean cost degradation, supported by per-attack curves and rollout storyboards.
本文针对去中心化多智能体路径规划（MAPF）策略在观测攻击下的脆弱性问题，即微小输入扰动会导致智能体碰撞和系统拥堵。作者提出了两种保持相同网络架构和部署流程的训练方案：Adv-PPO，通过对抗最坏情况扰动训练共享策略并依据对抗性能选择检查点；以及Adv-PPO+MACER，利用随机平滑认证半径的平滑项对Adv-PPO检查点进行微调。在8x8 POGEMA地图和四个智能体的实验中，未受保护的PPO策略在干净环境下成功率为95.8%，但在最强攻击下仅2.5%；Adv-PPO以1%的干净性能代价将最坏情况成功率恢复至59.2%，而Adv-PPO+MACER在三个独立种子下以不到1%的干净性能代价进一步提升至77.5% ± 6.0%，并通过逐攻击曲线和 rollout 故事板验证了结果。
Drop the Act: Probe-Filtered RL for Faithful Chain-of-Thought Reasoning
Authors: Swapnil Parekh
First: 2026-05-12T03:30:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T03:30:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reasoning models post-hoc rationalize answers they have already committed to internally, producing chains of *reasoning theater*: deliberative-looking steps that contribute nothing to correctness. This wastes inference tokens, pollutes interpretability, and obscures what the model actually computed. We introduce **ProFIL** (**Pro**be-**Fil**tered Reinforcement Learning) to *reduce theater, increase chain-of-thought faithfulness, and shrink chain length* in a single, drop-in extension to Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). A multi-head attention probe is trained *once* on the *frozen* base model to detect post-commitment steps from internal activations alone; during GRPO, rollouts whose probe score exceeds a threshold have their advantage zeroed. *Our central finding is that a probe trained on a frozen base, with verifier-derived labels and no human annotation, provides a stable signal that suppresses theater while resisting the RL-obfuscation failure mode predicted by prior work.* Across four reasoning domains (GSM8K, LiveCodeBench, ToolUse, MMLU-Redux) and two model architectures (Llama-8B, Qwen-7B), ProFIL reduces post-commitment theater by **11--100%**, raises faithful-fraction (e.g., +24pp on LiveCodeBench under an independent Claude 3.7 Sonnet judge), and shortens chains by 4--19%, all while preserving or improving task accuracy. ProFIL also beats a matched length-penalty GRPO baseline, isolating the gain as semantic commitment-detection rather than chain compression. Probe weights, training configurations, and rollouts are released across all four domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：放下伪装：基于探针过滤的强化学习实现忠实思维链推理
推理模型在事后对已内部确定的答案进行合理化解释，产生*推理表演*链条：看似深思熟虑的步骤对正确性毫无贡献。这浪费推理令牌、污染可解释性，并掩盖模型实际计算的内容。我们提出**ProFIL**（**探**针-**过**滤**强**化学习），作为组相对策略优化（GRPO）的即插即用扩展，旨在*减少表演、提升思维链忠实度、缩短链长度*。在*冻结*基模型上*一次性*训练多头注意力探针，仅从内部激活检测事后承诺步骤；在GRPO期间，探针得分超过阈值的展开序列其优势归零。*核心发现是：在冻结基模型上训练的探针，使用验证器派生标签且无需人工标注，能提供稳定信号抑制表演，同时抵御先前工作预测的RL混淆失效模式。*在四个推理领域（GSM8K、LiveCodeBench、ToolUse、MMLU-Redux）和两种模型架构（Llama-8B、Qwen-7B）上，ProFIL将事后承诺表演减少**11–100%**，提升忠实比例（例如在LiveCodeBench上独立Claude 3.7 Sonnet评判下+24个百分点），并将链长度缩短4–19%，同时保持或提升任务准确率。ProFIL还优于匹配的长度惩罚GRPO基线，将增益归因于语义承诺检测而非链压缩。探针权重、训练配置和展开序列已在所有四个领域发布。

Breaking $\textit{Winner-Takes-All}$: Cooperative Policy Optimization Improves Diverse LLM Reasoning
Authors: Haoxuan Chen, Tianming Liang, Wei-Shi Zheng, Jian-Fang Hu
First: 2026-05-12T03:20:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T03:20:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiers (RLVR) has become a central paradigm for improving LLM reasoning, yet popular group-based optimization algorithms like GRPO often suffer from exploration collapse, where the models prematurely converge on a narrow set of high-scoring patterns, lacking the ability to explore new solutions. Recent efforts attempt to alleviate this by adding entropy regularization or diversity bonus. However, these approaches do not change the \textit{winner-takes-all} nature, where rollouts still compete for individual advantage rather than cooperating for maximizing global diversity. In this work, we propose Group Cooperative Policy Optimization (GCPO), which shifts the training paradigm from rollout competition to team cooperation. Specifically, GCPO replaces independent rollout scoring with team-level credit assignment: a rollout is rewarded by how much it contributes to the team's valid solution coverage, rather than its individual accuracy. This coverage is described as a determinant volume over reward-weighted semantic embeddings, where only correct and non-redundant rollouts contribute to this volume. During advantage estimation, GCPO redistributes the collective team reward to each single rollout according to its average marginal contribution to the team. This cooperative training paradigm routes optimization toward non-redundant correct reasoning paths. Experiments across multiple reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that GCPO significantly improves both reasoning accuracy and solution diversity over existing approaches. Code will be released at $\href{https://github.com/bradybuddiemarch/gcpo}{this}$.
中文标题/摘要
标题：打破“赢家通吃”：合作策略优化提升大语言模型推理多样性
基于验证器的强化学习（RLVR）已成为提升大语言模型推理能力的核心范式，但GRPO等流行的群体优化算法常遭遇探索崩溃问题——模型过早收敛于少数高分模式，缺乏探索新解的能力。近期研究尝试通过添加熵正则化或多样性奖励来缓解此问题，但这些方法并未改变“赢家通吃”的本质，即采样结果仍为争夺个体优势而竞争，而非通过合作最大化全局多样性。本文提出群体合作策略优化（GCPO），将训练范式从采样竞争转向团队合作。具体而言，GCPO用团队级信用分配替代独立采样评分：采样结果根据其对团队有效解覆盖率的贡献获得奖励，而非其个体准确率。该覆盖率被定义为奖励加权语义嵌入的行列式体积，仅正确且非冗余的采样结果贡献于此体积。在优势估计阶段，GCPO根据每个采样结果对团队的平均边际贡献，将集体团队奖励重新分配给单个采样结果。这种合作训练范式引导优化朝向非冗余的正确推理路径。在多个推理基准上的实验表明，GCPO在推理准确率和解多样性上均显著优于现有方法。代码将发布于\href{https://github.com/bradybuddiemarch/gcpo}{此链接}。

The authors propose Group Cooperative Policy Optimization (GCPO), which shifts from a winner-takes-all competition among rollouts to a cooperative team framework, where each rollout is rewarded based on its marginal contribution to the team's coverage of valid, non-redundant solutions, measured via determinant volume over reward-weighted semantic embeddings. Experiments across multiple reasoning benchmarks show that GCPO significantly improves both reasoning accuracy and solution diversity compared to existing methods.
该论文针对基于验证器的强化学习（RLVR）中存在的探索崩溃问题，即GRPO等群体优化算法过早收敛于少数高分模式，缺乏探索新解的能力。作者提出群体协作策略优化（GCPO），将训练范式从胜者通吃的竞争转变为团队协作，每个轨迹根据其对团队有效且非冗余解覆盖的边际贡献获得奖励，该覆盖通过奖励加权语义嵌入的行列式体积衡量。在多个推理基准上的实验表明，GCPO在推理准确性和解多样性上均显著优于现有方法。
GESR: A Genetic Programming-Based Symbolic Regression Method with Gene Editing
Authors: Yanjie Li, Weijun Li, Xin Ning
First: 2026-05-11T15:00:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T03:13:44+00:00
Comments: 70 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Mathematical formulas serve as a language through which humans communicate with nature. Discovering mathematical laws from scientific data to describe natural phenomena has been a long-standing pursuit of humanity for centuries. In the field of artificial intelligence, this challenge is known as the symbolic regression problem. Among existing symbolic regression approaches, Genetic Programming (GP) based on evolutionary algorithms remains one of the most classical and widely adopted methods. GP simulates the evolutionary process across generations through genetic mutation and crossover. However, mutations and crossovers in GP are entirely random. While this randomness effectively mimics natural evolution, it inevitably produces both beneficial and detrimental variations. If there existed a metaphorical `God` capable of foreseeing which genetic mutations or crossovers would yield superior outcomes and performing targeted gene editing accordingly, the efficiency of evolution could be substantially improved. Motivated by this idea, we propose in this paper a symbolic regression approach based on gene editing, termed GESR. In GESR, we trained two "hands of God" (two BERT models). Among them, the first leverages the BERT's masked language modeling capability to guide the mutation of genes (expression symbols). The other BERT model guides the crossover of individual genes by predicting the crossover point. Experimental results demonstrate that GESR significantly improves computational efficiency compared with traditional GP algorithms and achieves strong overall performance across multiple symbolic regression tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GESR：一种基于基因编辑的遗传编程符号回归方法
数学公式是人类与自然沟通的语言。从科学数据中发现数学规律以描述自然现象，是人类数百年来长期追求的目标。在人工智能领域，这一挑战被称为符号回归问题。在现有的符号回归方法中，基于进化算法的遗传编程（GP）仍是最经典且广泛采用的方法之一。GP通过基因突变和交叉模拟跨代进化过程。然而，GP中的突变和交叉完全是随机的。这种随机性虽能有效模拟自然进化，但不可避免地会产生有益和有害的变异。如果存在一个隐喻性的“上帝”，能够预见哪些基因突变或交叉会产生更优结果，并据此进行靶向基因编辑，那么进化效率将大幅提升。受此启发，本文提出了一种基于基因编辑的符号回归方法，称为GESR。在GESR中，我们训练了两个“上帝之手”（两个BERT模型）。其中，第一个利用BERT的掩码语言建模能力来指导基因（表达式符号）的突变。另一个BERT模型通过预测交叉点来指导个体基因的交叉。实验结果表明，与传统GP算法相比，GESR显著提高了计算效率，并在多个符号回归任务中取得了优异的整体性能。

The method trains two BERT models as 'hands of God': one uses masked language modeling to guide gene mutations, and the other predicts crossover points to direct gene recombination. Experimental results show that GESR significantly improves computational efficiency over traditional GP and achieves strong overall performance across multiple symbolic regression tasks.
该论文提出了一种基于基因编辑的遗传编程符号回归方法GESR，其动机在于传统GP中随机突变和交叉的低效性。该方法训练了两个BERT模型作为“上帝之手”：一个利用掩码语言建模能力指导基因（表达式符号）的突变，另一个通过预测交叉点来指导基因重组。实验结果表明，与传统的GP算法相比，GESR显著提高了计算效率，并在多个符号回归任务中取得了优异的整体性能。
Asymmetric Advantage Modulation Calibrates Entropy Dynamics in RLVR
Authors: Hengrui Gu, Xiaotian Han, Yujing Bian, Feiyi Wang, Kaixiong Zhou
First: 2026-04-06T17:42:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T03:13:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has substantially improved the reasoning ability of large language models (LLMs), but it often suffers from \textit{restricted exploration}, where the policy rapidly concentrates on a narrow set of solutions. A common remedy is entropy regularization, which attempts to preserve exploration by increasing policy entropy. However, for LLM-RL, this intervention is highly sensitive to its coefficient, can introduce semantically weak uncertainty, and often yields limited accuracy gains. This motivates a more precise question: which entropy helps reasoning, and which entropy should be reduced? To study this, we parameterize the advantage estimator in Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) into positive and negative outcome-conditioned channels and analyze their entropy dynamics. Our results show that positive-channel modulation raises \textit{productive entropy} associated with successful reasoning trajectories, while negative-channel modulation removes \textit{noisy entropy} associated with failed rollouts and reduces interference with correct paths. Guided by this channel-wise view, we propose \textbf{AsymGRPO}, which decouples the modulation strengths of positive and negative advantages. This enables flexible control over how the model updates across prompt difficulty levels, allowing stronger reinforcement of rare successes on harder prompts or stronger suppression of residual failures on easier prompts without forcing the two channels to share the same modulation strength. Experiments on five mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that AsymGRPO outperforms strong RLVR baselines, with consistent gains across model backbones.
Summary / 总结
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) improves LLM reasoning but often causes restricted exploration, where the policy converges on a narrow solution set. To address this, the authors propose AsymGRPO, which decouples the modulation strengths of positive and negative advantages in Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), allowing separate control over productive entropy from successful trajectories and noisy entropy from failures. Experiments on five mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that AsymGRPO consistently outperforms strong RLVR baselines across different model backbones, achieving significant accuracy gains.
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）提升了大型语言模型的推理能力，但常导致策略快速收敛于狭窄解集，限制探索。为此，作者提出AsymGRPO方法，将GRPO中的优势估计分解为正负两个通道，分别调节成功轨迹的“生产性熵”和失败轨迹的“噪声熵”，从而灵活控制不同难度提示下的更新强度。在五个数学推理基准上的实验表明，AsymGRPO在多种模型骨干上均显著优于强RLVR基线，取得一致的准确率提升。
PiCA: Pivot-Based Credit Assignment for Search Agentic Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Dongyi Liu, Yifan Niu, Qinwen Wang, Han Xiao, Jia Li
First: 2026-05-10T03:21:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T03:05:01+00:00
Comments: 21 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large Language Model (LLM)-based search agents trained with reinforcement learning (RL) have significantly improved the performance of knowledge-intensive tasks. However, existing methods encounter critical challenges in long-horizon credit assignment: (i) Reward Sparsity, where models receive only outcome feedback without step-level guidance to differentiate action quality; (ii) Isolated Credit, where credit is assigned to steps independently, failing to capture sequential dependencies; and (iii) Distributional Shift, where rewards are estimated on templates that deviate from the model's natural generative distribution. To address these issues, we propose Pivot-Based Credit Assignment (PiCA), a novel step reward mechanism that reformulates the search trajectory as a sequential process of cumulative search progress. Unlike prior isolated step rewards, PiCA defines process rewards as success probabilities dependent on the historical context based on Potential-Based Reward Shaping (PBRS). This approach identifies pivot steps, which comprise target golden sub-queries and sub-answers derived from historical trajectories, as information peaks that significantly boost the likelihood of a correct final answer. By anchoring these step rewards to the final task objective, PiCA provides dense, pivot-aware and trajectory-dependent guidance while maintaining distributional consistency. Extensive experiments show that PiCA outperforms existing strong baselines across seven knowledge-intensive QA benchmarks, achieving 15.2% and 2.2% improvements for 3B and 7B models. The consistent performance gains across various models show PiCA's robust generalization. The code is available at https://github.com/novdream/PiCA.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PiCA：基于支点的搜索智能体强化学习信用分配方法
基于大语言模型的搜索智能体通过强化学习训练，显著提升了知识密集型任务的性能。然而，现有方法在长程信用分配中面临关键挑战：(i) 奖励稀疏性——模型仅接收结果反馈，缺乏区分动作质量的步骤级指导；(ii) 孤立信用——信用被独立分配给各步骤，未能捕捉序列依赖关系；(iii) 分布偏移——奖励在偏离模型自然生成分布的模板上进行估计。为解决这些问题，我们提出基于支点的信用分配方法（PiCA），这是一种新型步骤奖励机制，将搜索轨迹重构为累积搜索进度的序列过程。与先前孤立的步骤奖励不同，PiCA基于势能奖励塑形技术，将过程奖励定义为依赖历史上下文的成功概率。该方法识别出支点步骤——即由历史轨迹中提取的目标黄金子查询和子答案构成的信息峰值，这些步骤能显著提升最终正确答案的可能性。通过将这些步骤奖励锚定到最终任务目标，PiCA在保持分布一致性的同时，提供了密集、支点感知且轨迹依赖的指导。大量实验表明，PiCA在七个知识密集型问答基准上超越现有强基线，在3B和7B模型上分别实现15.2%和2.2%的性能提升。跨多种模型的一致性能增益证明了PiCA的稳健泛化能力。代码已开源：https://github.com/novdream/PiCA。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses credit assignment challenges in reinforcement learning for LLM-based search agents, specifically reward sparsity, isolated credit, and distributional shift. The authors propose PiCA, a pivot-based credit assignment method that reformulates search trajectories as cumulative progress and uses Potential-Based Reward Shaping to define process rewards as success probabilities dependent on historical context, identifying pivot steps as information peaks. Experiments on seven knowledge-intensive QA benchmarks show PiCA outperforms strong baselines, achieving 15.2% and 2.2% improvements for 3B and 7B models, with consistent generalization across models.
该论文针对基于强化学习的LLM搜索智能体在信用分配中面临的奖励稀疏、孤立信用和分布偏移问题，提出了基于支点的信用分配方法PiCA。该方法将搜索轨迹重构为累积进展过程，利用基于势能的奖励塑造将过程奖励定义为依赖历史上下文的成功概率，并识别支点步骤作为信息峰值。在七个知识密集型问答基准上的实验表明，PiCA优于现有强基线，在3B和7B模型上分别实现了15.2%和2.2%的提升，且在不同模型上表现出稳健的泛化能力。
Agent-BRACE: Decoupling Beliefs from Actions in Long-Horizon Tasks via Verbalized State Uncertainty
Authors: Joykirat Singh, Zaid Khan, Archiki Prasad, Justin Chih-Yao Chen, Akshay Nambi, Hyunji Lee, Elias Stengel-Eskin, Mohit Bansal
First: 2026-05-12T02:37:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T02:37:04+00:00
Comments: Code: https://github.com/joykirat18/Agent-BRACE
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed on long-horizon tasks in partially observable environments, where they must act while inferring and tracking a complex environment state over many steps. This leads to two challenges: partial observability requires maintaining uncertainty over unobserved world attributes, and long interaction history causes context to grow without bound, diluting task-relevant information. A principled solution to both challenges is a belief state: a posterior distribution over environment states given past observations and actions, which compactly encodes history for decision making regardless of episode length. In LLM agents, however, the open-ended nature of text makes it unclear how to represent such a distribution. Therefore, we introduce Agent-BRACE: Agent Belief state Representation via Abstraction and Confidence Estimation, a method that decouples an LLM agent into a belief state model and a policy model, jointly optimized via reinforcement learning. The belief state model produces a structured approximation of the belief distribution: a set of atomic natural language claims about the environment, each annotated with an ordinal verbalized certainty label ranging from certain to unknown. The policy model conditions on this compact, structured approximate belief rather than the full history, learning to select actions under explicit uncertainty. Across long-horizon, partially observable embodied language environments, Agent-BRACE achieves an average absolute improvement of +14.5% (Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct) and +5.3% (Qwen3-4B-Instruct), outperforming strong RL baselines while maintaining a near-constant context window independent of episode length. Further analysis shows that the learned belief becomes increasingly calibrated over the course of an episode as evidence accumulates.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Agent-BRACE：通过言语化状态不确定性在长时任务中解耦信念与行动
大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被部署在部分可观测环境中的长时任务上，它们必须在多个步骤中推断并跟踪复杂环境状态的同时采取行动。这带来了两个挑战：部分可观测性要求对未观测到的世界属性保持不确定性，而长交互历史会导致上下文无限增长，稀释任务相关信息。针对这两个挑战的一个原则性解决方案是信念状态：给定过去观测和行动的环境状态后验分布，它能够紧凑地编码历史以支持决策，无论情节长度如何。然而，在LLM智能体中，文本的开放性使得如何表示这种分布尚不明确。因此，我们引入Agent-BRACE：通过抽象和置信度估计的智能体信念状态表示，该方法将LLM智能体解耦为信念状态模型和策略模型，并通过强化学习联合优化。信念状态模型生成信念分布的结构化近似：一组关于环境的原子自然语言声明，每个声明都带有一个从确定到未知的有序言语化确定性标签。策略模型基于这种紧凑、结构化的近似信念（而非完整历史）进行条件化，学习在显式不确定性下选择行动。在长时、部分可观测的具身语言环境中，Agent-BRACE实现了平均绝对提升+14.5%（Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct）和+5.3%（Qwen3-4B-Instruct），优于强强化学习基线，同时保持与情节长度无关的近乎恒定的上下文窗口。进一步分析表明，随着证据积累，学习到的信念在情节过程中变得越来越校准。
Summary / 总结
Agent-BRACE addresses the challenges of partial observability and unbounded context in long-horizon tasks by decoupling an LLM agent into a belief state model and a policy model, jointly optimized via reinforcement learning. The belief model represents uncertainty through atomic natural language claims with ordinal verbalized certainty labels, while the policy conditions on this compact belief instead of full history. Experiments in embodied language environments show absolute improvements of +14.5% and +5.3% over strong RL baselines, with a constant context window independent of episode length and increasingly calibrated beliefs as evidence accumulates.
Agent-BRACE通过将LLM代理解耦为信念状态模型和策略模型（两者通过强化学习联合优化），解决了长周期任务中的部分可观测性和上下文无限增长问题。信念模型使用带有序数言语化确定性标签的原子自然语言声明来表示不确定性，策略则基于紧凑信念而非完整历史进行决策。在具身语言环境中的实验表明，该方法相比强强化学习基线取得了+14.5%和+5.3%的绝对提升，上下文窗口长度与回合长度无关，且信念随证据积累而逐渐校准。
Learning to Explore: Scaling Agentic Reasoning via Exploration-Aware Policy Optimization
Authors: Xingyuan Hua, Sheng Yue, Ju Ren
First: 2026-05-09T14:44:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T02:23:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recent advancements in agentic test-time scaling allow models to gather environmental feedback before committing to final actions. A key limitation of existing methods is that they typically employ undifferentiated exploration strategies, lacking the ability to adaptively distinguish when exploration is truly required. In this paper, we propose an exploration-aware reinforcement learning framework that enables LLM agents to adaptively explore only when uncertainty is high. Our method introduces a fine-grained reward function via variational inference that explicitly evaluates exploratory actions by estimating their potential to improve future decision-making, together with an exploration-aware grouping mechanism that separates exploratory actions from task-completion actions during optimization. By targeting informational gaps, this design allows agents to explore selectively and transition to execution as soon as the task context is clear. Empirically, we demonstrate that our approach achieves consistent improvements across a range of challenging text-based and GUI-based agent benchmarks. Code is available at https://github.com/HansenHua/EAPO-ICML26 and models are available at https://huggingface.co/hansenhua/EAPO-ICML26.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学会探索：通过探索感知策略优化扩展智能体推理
近期在智能体测试时扩展方面的进展使模型能够在确定最终行动前收集环境反馈。现有方法的一个关键局限在于它们通常采用无差别的探索策略，缺乏自适应判断何时真正需要探索的能力。本文提出一种探索感知的强化学习框架，使大语言模型智能体仅在不确定性高时进行自适应探索。我们的方法通过变分推断引入细粒度奖励函数，通过估计探索行动改善未来决策的潜力来显式评估它们，同时结合一种探索感知的分组机制，在优化过程中将探索行动与任务完成行动分离。通过针对信息缺口，该设计使智能体能够选择性探索，并在任务上下文清晰时立即转向执行。实验表明，我们的方法在一系列具有挑战性的基于文本和基于图形用户界面的智能体基准测试中均取得了一致改进。代码和模型分别见 https://github.com/HansenHua/EAPO-ICML26 和 https://huggingface.co/hansenhua/EAPO-ICML26。

The paper addresses the limitation of current agentic test-time scaling methods that use undifferentiated exploration strategies, lacking the ability to adaptively determine when exploration is necessary. The authors propose an exploration-aware reinforcement learning framework that enables LLM agents to explore selectively only when uncertainty is high, using a variational inference-based fine-grained reward function to evaluate exploratory actions and an exploration-aware grouping mechanism to separate exploration from task-completion during optimization. Empirical results show consistent improvements across challenging text-based and GUI-based agent benchmarks, demonstrating the effectiveness of the approach.
该论文针对当前智能体测试时扩展方法中采用无差别探索策略、缺乏自适应判断何时需要探索的局限性，提出了一种探索感知的强化学习框架，使大语言模型代理仅在不确定性高时进行选择性探索。该方法通过变分推断引入细粒度奖励函数来评估探索性行动对改善未来决策的潜力，并采用探索感知分组机制在优化过程中将探索行动与任务完成行动分离。实验结果表明，该方法在多个具有挑战性的基于文本和图形用户界面的智能体基准测试中均取得了一致的性能提升。
Vulnerable Agent Identification in Large-Scale Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Simin Li, Zihao Mao, Zheng Yuwei, Linhao Wang, Ruixiao Xu, Chengdong Ma, Zhiqian Liu, Xin Yu, Yuqing Ma, Xin Wang, Jie Luo, Bo An, Yaodong Yang, Weifeng Lv, Xianglong Liu
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2025-09-18T16:03:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T02:18:50+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Partial agent failure becomes inevitable when systems scale up, making it crucial to identify the subset of agents whose failure causes worst-case system performance degradations. We study this Vulnerable Agent Identification (VAI) problem in large-scale multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL). We frame VAI as a Hierarchical Adversarial Decentralized Mean Field Control (HAD-MFC), where the upper level selects vulnerable agents as an NP-hard task and the lower level learns their worst-case adversarial policies via mean-field MARL. The two problems are coupled together, making HAD-MFC difficult to solve. To handle this, we first decouple the hierarchical process by Fenchel-Rockafellar transform, resulting a regularized mean-field Bellman operator for upper level that enables independent learning at each level, thus reducing computational complexity. We next reformulate the upper-level NP-hard problem as an MDP with dense rewards, allowing sequential identification of vulnerable agents via greedy and RL algorithms. This decomposition provably preserves the optimal solution. Experiments show our method effectively identifies more vulnerable agents in large-scale MARL and the rule-based system, fooling system into worse failures, and reveals the vulnerability of each agent in large systems. Code available at https://github.com/Waken-dream/VAI
中文标题/摘要
标题：大规模多智能体强化学习中的脆弱智能体识别
当系统规模扩大时，部分智能体故障变得不可避免，因此识别那些导致系统性能最严重下降的智能体子集至关重要。我们研究了大规模多智能体强化学习（MARL）中的脆弱智能体识别（VAI）问题。我们将VAI建模为分层对抗性分散平均场控制（HAD-MFC），其中上层选择脆弱智能体（NP难任务），下层通过平均场MARL学习其最坏情况下的对抗策略。这两个问题相互耦合，使得HAD-MFC难以求解。为此，我们首先通过Fenchel-Rockafellar变换解耦分层过程，得到上层的正则化平均场Bellman算子，使各层能够独立学习，从而降低计算复杂度。接着，我们将上层的NP难问题重新表述为具有密集奖励的MDP，允许通过贪婪算法和RL算法顺序识别脆弱智能体。这种分解可证明地保留了最优解。实验表明，我们的方法能在大规模MARL和基于规则的系统中有效识别更多脆弱智能体，使系统陷入更严重的故障，并揭示大规模系统中每个智能体的脆弱性。代码见https://github.com/Waken-dream/VAI
fg-expo: Frontier-guided exploration-prioritized policy optimization via adaptive kl and gaussian curriculum
Authors: Mingxiong Lin, Zhangquan Gong, Maowen Tang, Qian Li, Chuangchuang Wang, Jian Ma, Sutian Huang, Kai Tang, Haonan Lu
First: 2026-05-12T01:48:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T01:48:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become the standard paradigm for LLM mathematical reasoning, with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) serving as the dominant algorithm. We identify two overlooked inefficiencies inherent in GRPO. First, a fixed KL coefficient overly restricts policy exploration at moments when the model needs to diverge significantly from the reference policy. Second, uniform question sampling overlooks that moderately difficult problems produce the most informative gradient signals. We propose FG-ExPO, short for Frontier-Guided Exploration-Prioritized Policy Optimization, which integrates two lightweight components. Accuracy-Conditioned KL Scaling (AKL) adjusts the KL penalty strength through a smooth nonlinear function of batch average accuracy, loosening the constraint when the model performs poorly and strengthening it when the model achieves satisfactory results. Gaussian Curriculum Sampling (GCS) assigns sampling weights to questions following a Gaussian distribution centered at a moderate accuracy level around 0.5, focusing model training on its learning frontier. We conduct evaluations on DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B and Qwen3-8B-Base across six mainstream mathematical reasoning benchmarks. Experimental results demonstrate that FG-ExPO consistently outperforms vanilla GRPO. It delivers an absolute improvement of 13.34 on the AIME 2025 pass@32 metric, rising from 63.33 percent to 76.67 percent, and obtains an average pass@32 gain of 2.66 on the 8B model. The substantially larger performance gains observed on pass@32 compared to pass@1 verify that FG-ExPO enlarges the model's effective exploration space under a fixed inference budget.
中文标题/摘要
标题：fg-expo：基于自适应KL与高斯课程的前沿引导探索优先策略优化
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为大语言模型数学推理的标准范式，其中群体相对策略优化（GRPO）是主流算法。我们识别出GRPO中两个被忽视的低效问题：首先，固定KL系数在模型需要显著偏离参考策略时过度限制策略探索；其次，均匀问题采样忽略了中等难度问题能产生最具信息量的梯度信号。为此提出FG-ExPO（前沿引导探索优先策略优化），集成两个轻量组件：精度条件KL缩放（AKL）通过批次平均精度的平滑非线性函数调整KL惩罚强度，在模型表现差时放松约束、表现好时加强约束；高斯课程采样（GCS）以0.5附近中等精度水平为中心的高斯分布分配问题采样权重，聚焦模型训练于其学习前沿。在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B和Qwen3-8B-Base上，基于六个主流数学推理基准的评估表明，FG-ExPO持续优于原始GRPO：在AIME 2025的pass@32指标上实现13.34的绝对提升（从63.33%升至76.67%），在8B模型上平均pass@32增益达2.66。pass@32相比pass@1的显著更大性能增益验证了FG-ExPO在固定推理预算下扩大了模型的有效探索空间。
Summary / 总结
The paper identifies two inefficiencies in Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) for reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards: a fixed KL coefficient that overly restricts exploration and uniform question sampling that neglects the most informative gradient signals from moderately difficult problems. To address these, the authors propose FG-ExPO, which integrates Accuracy-Conditioned KL Scaling (AKL) to dynamically adjust the KL penalty based on batch accuracy, and Gaussian Curriculum Sampling (GCS) to prioritize questions near a moderate accuracy level of 0.5. Evaluated on DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B and Qwen3-8B-Base across six mathematical reasoning benchmarks, FG-ExPO consistently outperforms vanilla GRPO, achieving a 13.34% absolute improvement on AIME 2025 pass@32 (from 63.33% to 76.67%) and an average pass@32 gain of 2.66 on the 8B model, with larger gains on pass@32 than pass@1 indicating expanded effective exploration space.
该论文指出Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO)在可验证奖励的强化学习中存在两个被忽视的低效问题：固定的KL系数过度限制了模型需要大幅偏离参考策略时的探索，以及均匀的问题采样忽略了中等难度问题提供的最具信息量的梯度信号。为此，作者提出FG-ExPO方法，通过准确率条件KL缩放（AKL）根据批次平均准确率动态调整KL惩罚强度，以及高斯课程采样（GCS）将采样权重集中在准确率约0.5的中等难度问题上。在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B和Qwen3-8B-Base上对六个数学推理基准的评估显示，FG-ExPO持续优于原始GRPO，在AIME 2025的pass@32指标上实现13.34%的绝对提升（从63.33%升至76.67%），并在8B模型上获得平均2.66的pass@32增益，且pass@32上的更大提升验证了该方法在固定推理预算下扩大了模型的有效探索空间。
Behavioral Mode Discovery for Fine-tuning Multimodal Generative Policies
Authors: Alberta Longhini, David Emukpere, Jean-Michel Renders, Seungsu Kim
Venue: International Conference on Machine Learning, 2026
First: 2026-05-12T01:19:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T01:19:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We address the problem of fine-tuning pre-trained generative policies with reinforcement learning (RL) while preserving the multimodality of their action distributions. Existing methods for RL fine-tuning of generative policies (e.g., diffusion policies) improve task performance but often collapse diverse behaviors into a single reward-maximizing mode. To mitigate this issue, we propose an unsupervised mode discovery framework that uncovers latent behavioral modes within generative policies. The discovered modes enable the use of mutual information as an intrinsic reward, regularizing RL fine-tuning to enhance task success while maintaining behavioral diversity. Experiments on robotic manipulation tasks demonstrate that our method consistently outperforms conventional fine-tuning approaches, achieving higher success rates and preserving richer multimodal action distributions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向多模态生成策略微调的行为模式发现
我们解决了在保持生成策略动作分布多模态性的同时，通过强化学习（RL）微调预训练生成策略的问题。现有生成策略（如扩散策略）的RL微调方法虽能提升任务性能，但常将多样行为坍缩至单一奖励最大化模式。为缓解此问题，我们提出一种无监督模式发现框架，可揭示生成策略中的潜在行为模式。所发现的模式使互信息可作为内在奖励，通过正则化RL微调在增强任务成功率的同时维持行为多样性。机器人操作实验表明，我们的方法持续优于传统微调方法，实现了更高成功率并保留了更丰富的多模态动作分布。

Experiments on robotic manipulation tasks show that their method consistently outperforms conventional fine-tuning approaches, achieving higher success rates and preserving richer multimodal action distributions.
本文针对使用强化学习微调预训练生成策略时，现有方法常将多样行为坍缩为单一奖励最大化模式的问题，提出了一种无监督模式发现框架，该框架能揭示生成策略中的潜在行为模式，并利用互信息作为内在奖励来正则化强化学习微调过程，以在提升任务成功率的同时保持行为多样性。在机器人操作任务上的实验表明，该方法在成功率和保持多模态动作分布方面均持续优于传统微调方法。
Understanding the Performance Gap in Preference Learning: A Dichotomy of RLHF and DPO
Authors: Ruizhe Shi, Minhak Song, Runlong Zhou, Zihan Zhang, Maryam Fazel, Simon S. Du
Venue: ICML
First: 2025-05-26T09:54:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T01:02:19+00:00
Comments: ICML accepted version
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present a fine-grained theoretical analysis of the performance gap between two-stage reinforcement learning from human feedback~(RLHF) and direct preference optimization~(DPO). Our study decomposes this gap into two sources: the explicit representation gap under exact optimization and the implicit representation gap under finite samples. In the exact optimization setting, we characterize how the relative capacities of the reward and policy model classes influence the final policy qualities. We show that RLHF, DPO, or online DPO can outperform one another depending on type of model mis-specifications. Notably, online DPO can outperform both RLHF and standard DPO when the reward and policy model classes are isomorphic and both mis-specified. In the approximate optimization setting, we provide a concrete construction where the ground-truth reward is sparse and show that RLHF requires significantly fewer samples than DPO to recover an effective reward model, highlighting a statistical advantage of two-stage learning. Together, these results provide a comprehensive understanding of the performance gap between RLHF and DPO under various settings, and offer practical insights into when each method is preferred.
中文标题/摘要
标题：理解偏好学习中的性能差距：RLHF与DPO的二分法
我们对两阶段人类反馈强化学习（RLHF）与直接偏好优化（DPO）之间的性能差距进行了细粒度理论分析。研究将这一差距分解为两个来源：精确优化下的显式表示差距和有限样本下的隐式表示差距。在精确优化设置中，我们刻画了奖励模型类与策略模型类的相对容量如何影响最终策略质量。研究表明，根据模型误设类型的不同，RLHF、DPO或在线DPO可能各自表现更优。值得注意的是，当奖励与策略模型类同构且均存在误设时，在线DPO可同时优于RLHF和标准DPO。在近似优化设置中，我们构建了真实奖励稀疏的具体场景，证明RLHF恢复有效奖励模型所需的样本量显著少于DPO，凸显了两阶段学习的统计优势。这些结果共同提供了对RLHF与DPO在不同设置下性能差距的全面理解，并为每种方法的适用场景提供了实践指导。
Summary / 总结
This paper presents a theoretical analysis of the performance gap between reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) and direct preference optimization (DPO), decomposing it into explicit representation gaps under exact optimization and implicit representation gaps under finite samples. The method characterizes how the relative capacities of reward and policy model classes influence final policy qualities, showing that RLHF, DPO, or online DPO can outperform each other depending on model mis-specifications, with online DPO excelling when reward and policy classes are isomorphic and both mis-specified. In approximate optimization, the authors construct a sparse ground-truth reward scenario, demonstrating that RLHF requires significantly fewer samples than DPO to recover an effective reward model, highlighting a statistical advantage of two-stage learning.
本文对基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）与直接偏好优化（DPO）之间的性能差距进行了细粒度理论分析，将其分解为精确优化下的显式表示差距和有限样本下的隐式表示差距。该方法刻画了奖励模型类与策略模型类的相对容量如何影响最终策略质量，表明RLHF、DPO或在线DPO的性能优劣取决于模型误设类型，其中当奖励和策略类同构且均被误设时，在线DPO可优于两者。在近似优化场景中，作者构建了稀疏真实奖励的实例，证明RLHF比DPO需要显著更少的样本即可恢复有效奖励模型，突显了两阶段学习的统计优势。
gym-invmgmt: An Open Benchmarking Framework for Inventory Management Methods
Authors: Reza Barati, Qinmin Vivian Hu
First: 2026-05-12T00:22:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T00:22:15+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Inventory-policy comparisons are often difficult to interpret because performance depends on the evaluation contract as much as on the policy itself. Differences in topology, demand regime, information access, feasibility constraints, shortage treatment, and Key Performance Indicator (KPI) definitions can change method rankings. We present gym-invmgmt, a Gymnasium-compatible extension of the OR-Gym inventory-management lineage for auditable cross-paradigm evaluation. The benchmark evaluates optimization, heuristic, and learned controllers under a shared CoreEnv transition, reward, action-bound, and KPI contract, while varying stress conditions through a 22-scenario core grid plus four supplemental MARL-mode rows. Within these released scenarios, informed stochastic programming provides the strongest non-oracle reference, reflecting the value of scenario hedging under forecast access, but at substantially higher online computational cost. Among learned controllers, the Proximal Policy Optimization Transformer variant (PPO-Transformer) achieves the strongest learned-policy quality at fast inference, while Residual Reinforcement Learning (Residual RL) provides competitive hybrid performance. The graph neural network variant (PPO-GNN) is highly competitive on the default divergent topology but less robust on the serial topology. Imitation learning performs well in stationary regimes but degrades under demand shift, and the bounded Large Language Model (LLM) policy-parameter baseline is best interpreted as a diagnostic controller rather than an autonomous inventory optimizer. Overall, the benchmark identifies scenario-conditioned leaders while showing that performance depends jointly on information access, demand shift, topology, and policy representation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：gym-invmgmt：库存管理方法的开放基准测试框架
库存策略比较往往难以解读，因为性能既取决于策略本身，也取决于评估合约。拓扑结构、需求模式、信息获取、可行性约束、短缺处理以及关键绩效指标（KPI）定义的差异，都可能改变方法排名。我们提出gym-invmgmt，这是OR-Gym库存管理系列的一个兼容Gymnasium的扩展，用于可审计的跨范式评估。该基准测试在共享的CoreEnv转换、奖励、动作边界和KPI合约下评估优化、启发式和学习的控制器，同时通过22个场景核心网格加上四个补充的MARL模式行来改变压力条件。在这些已发布的场景中，知情随机规划提供了最强的非预言参考，反映了在预测获取下情景对冲的价值，但在线计算成本显著更高。在学习控制器中，近端策略优化Transformer变体（PPO-Transformer）在快速推理下实现了最强的学习策略质量，而残差强化学习（Residual RL）提供了有竞争力的混合性能。图神经网络变体（PPO-GNN）在默认发散拓扑上极具竞争力，但在串行拓扑上鲁棒性较差。模仿学习在平稳需求模式下表现良好，但在需求转移下性能下降，而有界大语言模型（LLM）策略参数基线最好被解释为诊断控制器，而非自主库存优化器。总体而言，该基准测试识别了场景条件下的领先者，同时表明性能共同依赖于信息获取、需求转移、拓扑结构和策略表示。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces gym-invmgmt, an open benchmarking framework for inventory management methods, motivated by the difficulty of comparing policies due to varying evaluation contracts. The framework extends OR-Gym to provide a shared CoreEnv transition, reward, action-bound, and KPI contract, evaluating optimization, heuristic, and learned controllers across 22 core scenarios plus MARL modes. Key results show that informed stochastic programming achieves the strongest non-oracle performance but with high computational cost, while among learned controllers, PPO-Transformer offers the best learned-policy quality with fast inference, Residual RL provides competitive hybrid performance, and PPO-GNN excels on divergent topologies but is less robust on serial ones, with imitation learning degrading under demand shift and LLM policies serving as diagnostic tools.

Epistemic Uncertainty for Test-Time Discovery
Authors: Kainat Riaz, Muhammad Ahmed Mohsin, Ahsan Bilal, Muhammad Umer, Ayesha Mohsin, Aqib Riaz, Ali Subhan, John M. Cioffi
First: 2026-05-11T23:26:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T23:26:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Automated scientific discovery using large language models relies on identifying genuinely novel solutions. Standard reinforcement learning penalizes high-variance mutations, which leads the policy to prioritize familiar patterns. As a result, the maximum reward plateaus even as the average reward increases. Overcoming this limitation requires a signal that distinguishes unexplored regions from intrinsically difficult problems. This necessitates measuring disagreement across independently adapted weight hypotheses rather than relying on a single network's confidence. UG-TTT addresses this challenge by maintaining a small ensemble of low-rank adapters over a frozen base model. The per-token disagreement, quantified as the mutual information between ensemble predictions and weight hypotheses, isolates epistemic uncertainty and identifies positions where insufficient coverage leads to adapter divergence rather than intrinsic problem difficulty. This measure is incorporated as an exploration bonus into the policy gradient, directing the policy toward positions where persistent adapter disagreement signals low training coverage, the same frontier where genuine discovery is possible. A nuclear norm regularizer ensures the adapters remain distinct from one another, thereby preserving the exploration signal throughout training. Across four scientific discovery benchmarks, UG-TTT increases the maximum reward on three tasks, maintains substantially higher solution diversity, and an ablation study confirms that the regularizer is essential for sustaining this behavior.
中文标题/摘要
标题：测试时发现的认知不确定性
利用大型语言模型进行自动化科学发现依赖于识别真正新颖的解决方案。标准强化学习会惩罚高变异突变，导致策略优先考虑熟悉模式。结果，即使平均奖励增加，最大奖励也会趋于平稳。克服这一限制需要一个能够区分未探索区域与内在困难问题的信号。这需要测量独立适应的权重假设之间的分歧，而非依赖单一网络的置信度。UG-TTT通过在冻结的基础模型上维护一个小型低秩适配器集成来解决这一挑战。每个令牌的分歧量化为集成预测与权重假设之间的互信息，从而隔离认知不确定性，并识别出因覆盖不足导致适配器发散而非问题本身困难的位置。该度量作为探索奖励纳入策略梯度，引导策略朝向适配器持续分歧指示训练覆盖不足的位置——这正是真正发现可能的前沿。核范数正则化器确保适配器彼此保持区分，从而在整个训练过程中维持探索信号。在四个科学发现基准测试中，UG-TTT在三个任务上提高了最大奖励，保持了显著更高的解决方案多样性，且消融研究证实正则化器对于维持这一行为至关重要。

To overcome this, the authors propose UG-TTT, which maintains a small ensemble of low-rank adapters over a frozen base model and uses per-token mutual information between ensemble predictions and weight hypotheses to isolate epistemic uncertainty, incorporating this as an exploration bonus into the policy gradient. A nuclear norm regularizer keeps adapters distinct. 该论文指出，标准强化学习在使用大型语言模型进行自动化科学发现时，会惩罚高变异性的突变，导致策略偏向熟悉模式，使得最大奖励在平均奖励增加时停滞不前。为解决此问题，作者提出UG-TTT方法，在冻结的基础模型上维护一个小型低秩适配器集成，利用集成预测与权重假设之间的逐令牌互信息来隔离认知不确定性，并将其作为探索奖励纳入策略梯度。核范数正则化器确保适配器保持差异。在四个科学发现基准上的实验表明，UG-TTT在三个任务上提升了最大奖励，保持了显著更高的解决方案多样性，且消融研究证实正则化器对维持此行为至关重要。
Quotient-Categorical Representations for Bellman-Compatible Average-Reward Distributional Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ege C. Kaya, Aliasghar Pourghani, Vijay Gupta, Abolfazl Hashemi
First: 2026-05-11T22:17:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T22:17:09+00:00
Comments: 29 pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Average-reward reinforcement learning requires estimating the gain and the bias, which is defined only up to an additive constant. This makes direct distributional analogues ill-posed on the real line. We introduce a quotient-space formulation in which state-indexed bias laws are identified up to a common translation, together with a categorical parameterization that respects this symmetry. On this quotient-categorical space, we define a projected average-reward distributional operator and show that it is well-defined, non-expansive in a coordinate Cramér metric, and admits fixed points. We then study sampled recursions whose mean-field maps are asynchronous relaxations of this operator. In an idealized centered-reward setting, a one-state temporal-difference update enjoys almost sure convergence together with finite-iteration residual bounds under both i.i.d. and Markovian sampling. When the gain is unknown, we augment the recursion with an online gain estimator, and prove non-expansiveness and Markovian convergence of the resulting coupled scheme. Finally, we show that synchronous exact updates are gain-independent at the quotient-law level, isolating a structural contrast between ideal quotient distributions and practical fixed-grid categorical representations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向平均奖励分布强化学习的商-分类表示
平均奖励强化学习需要估计增益和偏差，而偏差仅定义到加法常数。这使得直接的分布类比在实数轴上不适定。我们引入了一种商空间公式，其中状态索引的偏差律在共同平移下被识别，同时采用尊重这种对称性的分类参数化。在此商分类空间上，我们定义了一个投影平均奖励分布算子，并证明其良定义、在坐标Cramér度量下非扩张且存在不动点。随后我们研究了采样递归，其平均场映射是该算子的异步松弛。在理想化的中心奖励设定中，单状态时序差分更新在独立同分布和马尔可夫采样下均几乎必然收敛，并具有有限迭代残差界。当增益未知时，我们通过在线增益估计器增强递归，并证明所得耦合方案的非扩张性和马尔可夫收敛性。最后，我们证明同步精确更新在商律层面上与增益无关，从而揭示了理想商分布与实用固定网格分类表示之间的结构对比。

The authors propose a quotient-space formulation that identifies state-indexed bias laws up to a common translation, paired with a categorical parameterization respecting this symmetry. They define a projected average-reward distributional operator on this quotient-categorical space, proving it is well-defined, non-expansive in a coordinate Cramér metric, and admits fixed points. In an idealized centered-reward setting, a one-state temporal-difference update achieves almost sure convergence with finite-iteration residual bounds under both i.i.d. and Markovian sampling. When the gain is unknown, an online gain estimator is integrated, and the coupled scheme is shown to be non-expansive with Markovian convergence. On Training in Imagination
Authors: Nadav Timor, Ravid Shwartz-Ziv, Micah Goldblum, Yann LeCun, David Harel
First: 2026-05-07T12:51:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T21:19:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
State-of-the-art model-based reinforcement learning methods train policies on imagined rollouts. These rollouts are trajectories generated by a learned dynamics model and are scored by a learned reward model, but without querying the true environment during policy updates. We study this training paradigm by quantifying how errors in learned dynamics and reward models affect returns and policy optimization. First, we extend the analysis of Asadi et al. (2018) to MDPs with learned reward models, and derive the optimal sample allocation--the ratio of dynamics samples to reward samples that minimizes a bound on return error under power-law scaling assumptions. We identify lower Lipschitz constants of the learned dynamics, reward, and policy as a representation desideratum that tightens this bound, and we connect this perspective to the temporal-straightening objective of Wang et al. (2026). Second, we examine how policy optimization with REINFORCE tolerates noisy rewards, which are often cheaper to obtain. We show that zero-mean reward noise leaves the gradient estimator unbiased and adds at most a variance term that decreases with the number of rollouts. This introduces a practical tradeoff: given a fixed budget, should one buy more rollouts with cheaper but noisier rewards, or fewer rollouts with more expensive but less noisy rewards? We reduce this choice to a one-dimensional optimization problem and characterize the optimum.
Summary / 总结
This paper studies model-based reinforcement learning where policies are trained on imagined rollouts from learned dynamics and reward models without querying the true environment. The authors extend prior analysis to MDPs with learned reward models, deriving the optimal sample allocation between dynamics and reward samples to minimize a bound on return error under power-law scaling, and identify lower Lipschitz constants as a key representation property. They also analyze policy optimization with REINFORCE under noisy rewards, showing zero-mean noise leaves the gradient unbiased while adding variance that decreases with more rollouts, leading to a practical tradeoff between using cheaper noisier rewards for more rollouts versus expensive cleaner rewards for fewer rollouts, which they reduce to a one-dimensional optimization problem.
本文研究基于模型的强化学习中，策略在由学习到的动力学模型和奖励模型生成的想象轨迹上进行训练，而不查询真实环境。作者将先前分析扩展到具有学习奖励模型的MDP，推导出在幂律缩放假设下最小化回报误差界限的最优样本分配比例，并指出较低的动力学、奖励和策略的Lipschitz常数是收紧该界限的关键表示特性。他们还分析了在噪声奖励下使用REINFORCE进行策略优化的情况，表明零均值噪声不会使梯度估计产生偏差，但会引入随轨迹数量增加而减少的方差，从而产生一个实际权衡：在固定预算下，是使用更便宜但有噪声的奖励获取更多轨迹，还是使用更昂贵但噪声更小的奖励获取更少轨迹，他们将该选择简化为一个一维优化问题。
KEPO: Knowledge-Enhanced Preference Optimization for Multimodal Reasoning with Applications to Medical VQA
Authors: Fan Yang, Rui Meng, Trudi Di Qi, Ali Ezzati, Yuxin Wen
First: 2026-01-30T23:28:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T21:10:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a promising paradigm for inducing explicit reasoning behaviors in large language and vision-language models. However, reasoning-oriented RL post-training remains fundamentally challenging due to sparse trajectory-level rewards, leading to ambiguous credit assignment and severe exploration failures that can trap the policy in a ``learning cliff.'' Recent on-policy distillation methods introduce dense teacher supervision to stabilize optimization, but apply it uniformly across all generated trajectories. We argue that such uniform distillation is ill-suited for reasoning-intensive tasks, as low-quality on-policy trajectories often originate from early logical errors, and distillation under flawed contexts injects noisy and misaligned gradients. To address these challenges, we propose Knowledge-Enhanced Preference Optimization (KEPO), a unified post-training framework that integrates: (i) a quality-gated on-policy distillation objective that selectively applies dense teacher guidance only to high-quality trajectories, and (ii) a knowledge-enhanced exploration strategy that leverages hints learned from a teacher model to rejectively sample reward-positive on-policy trajectories for RL, thereby mitigating exploration collapse. Evaluated on a challenging medical visual question answering benchmark under single-source generalization, KEPO demonstrates improved training stability, more coherent reasoning behaviors, and superior out-of-distribution performance over reinforcement learning and on-policy distillation baselines.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses challenges in reinforcement learning for multimodal reasoning, particularly sparse rewards causing exploration failures. The authors propose Knowledge-Enhanced Preference Optimization (KEPO), a unified post-training framework with two key components: a quality-gated on-policy distillation objective that applies dense teacher guidance only to high-quality trajectories, and a knowledge-enhanced exploration strategy that uses teacher hints to rejectively sample reward-positive trajectories. Evaluated on a medical visual question answering benchmark under single-source generalization, KEPO achieves improved training stability, more coherent reasoning, and superior out-of-distribution performance compared to reinforcement learning and on-policy distillation baselines.
该论文针对多模态推理中强化学习面临的稀疏奖励导致探索失败的问题，提出了知识增强偏好优化（KEPO）框架。该框架包含两个核心组件：一是质量门控的在线策略蒸馏目标，仅对高质量轨迹应用密集的教师指导；二是知识增强的探索策略，利用教师模型的提示拒绝性地采样奖励为正的在线策略轨迹。在医学视觉问答基准上的单源泛化评估中，KEPO相比强化学习和在线策略蒸馏基线，展现出更优的训练稳定性、更连贯的推理行为以及更强的分布外性能。
Support-Proximity Augmented Diffusion Estimation for Offline Black-Box Optimization
Authors: Yonghan Yang, Ye Yuan, Zipeng Sun, Linfeng Du, Bowei He, Haolun Wu, Can Chen, Xue Liu
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-05-11T21:09:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T21:09:28+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline black-box optimization aims to discover novel designs with high property scores using only a static dataset, a task fundamentally challenged by the out-of-distribution (OOD) extrapolation problem. Existing approaches typically bifurcate into inverse methods, which struggle with the ill-posed nature of mapping scores to designs, and forward methods, which often lack the distributional expressivity to quantify uncertainty effectively. In this work, we propose SPADE (Support-Proximity Augmented Diffusion Estimation), a novel framework that reimagines forward surrogate modeling through the lens of conditional generative modeling. SPADE models the forward likelihood p(y|x) using a diffusion model, but with two critical enhancements to tailor it for optimization: (1) a Calibrated Diffusion Estimation module that enforces global consistency in statistical moments and pairwise rankings, and (2) a Support-Proximity Regularization mechanism that implicitly internalizes the data manifold constraint p(x) via kNN-based density estimation. Theoretically, we prove that our regularization is first-order equivalent to maximizing a Bayesian posterior with a valid design prior. Empirically, SPADE achieves state-of-the-art performance across Design-Bench tasks and an LLM data mixture optimization benchmark.
中文标题/摘要
标题：支持邻近增强扩散估计用于离线黑箱优化
离线黑箱优化旨在仅使用静态数据集发现具有高属性分数的新颖设计，这一任务从根本上受到分布外（OOD）外推问题的挑战。现有方法通常分为逆方法和前向方法：逆方法难以处理将分数映射到设计的不适定问题，而前向方法往往缺乏分布表达能力以有效量化不确定性。在这项工作中，我们提出SPADE（支持邻近增强扩散估计），这是一个通过条件生成建模视角重新构想前向代理建模的新框架。SPADE使用扩散模型对前向似然p(y|x)进行建模，但通过两项关键增强使其适用于优化：（1）校准扩散估计模块，强制统计矩和成对排序的全局一致性；（2）支持邻近正则化机制，通过基于k近邻的密度估计隐式内化数据流形约束p(x)。理论上，我们证明该正则化在优化中与最大化具有有效设计先验的贝叶斯后验一阶等价。实验上，SPADE在Design-Bench任务和LLM数据混合优化基准上实现了最先进的性能。
Summary / 总结
SPADE addresses the out-of-distribution extrapolation problem in offline black-box optimization by proposing a forward surrogate modeling framework based on conditional diffusion models. The method introduces two key enhancements: a Calibrated Diffusion Estimation module that ensures global consistency in statistical moments and pairwise rankings, and a Support-Proximity Regularization mechanism that implicitly enforces the data manifold constraint via kNN-based density estimation, which is theoretically proven to be first-order equivalent to maximizing a Bayesian posterior with a valid design prior. Empirically, SPADE achieves state-of-the-art performance across Design-Bench tasks and an LLM data mixture optimization benchmark.
SPADE针对离线黑盒优化中的分布外外推问题，提出了一种基于条件扩散模型的前向代理建模框架。该方法包含两个关键增强：校准扩散估计模块确保统计矩和成对排序的全局一致性，以及支持邻近正则化机制通过kNN密度估计隐式施加数据流形约束，理论上证明该正则化与使用有效设计先验最大化贝叶斯后验一阶等价。实验结果表明，SPADE在Design-Bench任务和LLM数据混合优化基准上均达到了最先进的性能。
Intention-Conditioned Flow Occupancy Models
Authors: Chongyi Zheng, Seohong Park, Sergey Levine, Benjamin Eysenbach
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-06-10T15:27:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T20:21:12+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3 · Project1
Abstract
Large-scale pre-training has fundamentally changed how machine learning research is done today: large foundation models are trained once, and then can be used by anyone in the community (including those without data or compute resources to train a model from scratch) to adapt and fine-tune to specific tasks. Applying this same framework to reinforcement learning (RL) is appealing because it offers compelling avenues for addressing core challenges in RL, including sample efficiency and robustness. However, there remains a fundamental challenge to pre-train large models in the context of RL: actions have long-term dependencies, so training a foundation model that reasons across time is important. Recent advances in generative AI have provided new tools for modeling highly complex distributions. In this paper, we build a probabilistic model to predict which states an agent will visit in the temporally distant future (i.e., an occupancy measure) using flow matching. As large datasets are often constructed by many distinct users performing distinct tasks, we include in our model a latent variable capturing the user intention. This intention increases the expressivity of our model, and enables adaptation with generalized policy improvement. We call our proposed method intention-conditioned flow occupancy models (InFOM). Comparing with alternative methods for pre-training, our experiments on $36$ state-based and $4$ image-based benchmark tasks demonstrate that the proposed method achieves $1.8 \times$ median improvement in returns and increases success rates by $36\%$. Website: https://chongyi-zheng.github.io/infom Code: https://github.com/chongyi-zheng/infom
中文标题/摘要
标题：意图条件流占用模型
大规模预训练从根本上改变了当今机器学习研究的方式：大型基础模型经过一次训练后，可供社区中的任何人（包括那些没有数据或计算资源从头训练模型的人）使用，以适应和微调特定任务。将同样的框架应用于强化学习（RL）具有吸引力，因为它为解决RL中的核心挑战（包括样本效率和鲁棒性）提供了引人注目的途径。然而，在RL背景下预训练大型模型仍面临一个根本性挑战：动作具有长期依赖性，因此训练一个跨时间推理的基础模型至关重要。生成式AI的最新进展为建模高度复杂的分布提供了新工具。在本文中，我们构建了一个概率模型，利用流匹配来预测智能体在时间上遥远的未来将访问哪些状态（即占用度量）。由于大型数据集通常由许多不同的用户执行不同的任务构建而成，我们在模型中包含了一个捕捉用户意图的潜在变量。该意图增强了我们模型的表达能力，并支持通过广义策略改进进行适应。我们将提出的方法称为意图条件流占用模型（InFOM）。与替代的预训练方法相比，我们在36个基于状态和4个基于图像的基准任务上的实验表明，所提出的方法在回报上实现了1.8倍的中位数改进，并将成功率提高了36%。网站：https://chongyi-zheng.github.io/infom 代码：https://github.com/chongyi-zheng/infom
