The paper addresses the challenge of pre-training large models for reinforcement learning, where actions have long-term dependencies that require temporal reasoning. The authors propose Intention-Conditioned Flow Occupancy Models (InFOM), a probabilistic model that uses flow matching to predict which states an agent will visit in the distant future, incorporating a latent variable for user intention to enhance expressivity and enable adaptation via generalized policy improvement. Experiments on 36 state-based and 4 image-based benchmark tasks show that InFOM achieves a 1.8x median improvement in returns and a 36% increase in success rates compared to alternative pre-training methods.
该论文针对强化学习中预训练大模型面临的挑战，即动作具有长期依赖性，需要跨时间推理。作者提出了意图条件流占用模型（InFOM），这是一种利用流匹配预测智能体在未来较远时间将访问哪些状态的概率模型，并通过引入潜在变量捕捉用户意图来增强模型表达能力，支持基于广义策略改进的适应。在36个基于状态和4个基于图像的基准任务上的实验表明，与替代预训练方法相比，InFOM实现了1.8倍的中位回报提升和36%的成功率增长。
Focusing Influence Mechanism for Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yisak Park, Sunwoo Lee, Seungyul Han
First: 2025-06-24T08:35:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T20:15:11+00:00
Comments: 9 technical page followed by references and appendix
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) under sparse rewards remains fundamentally challenging because agents often fail to concentrate their influence, leading to insufficiently coordinated exploration. To address this, we propose the Focusing Influence Mechanism (FIM), a framework that encourages agents to focus their influence on under-explored parts of the state space through an entropy-based criterion, while leveraging eligibility traces to enable multiple agents to consistently align and sustain their influence on the same parts of the state space when beneficial, thereby promoting coordinated and persistent joint behavior. By emphasizing under-explored regions of the state space, FIM facilitates more efficient and structured exploration even under extremely sparse rewards. Across diverse MARL benchmarks, FIM consistently improves cooperative performance over strong baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多智能体强化学习中的影响力聚焦机制
在稀疏奖励条件下，合作式多智能体强化学习仍面临根本性挑战，因为智能体往往无法集中其影响力，导致协调探索不足。为此，我们提出影响力聚焦机制（FIM），该框架通过基于熵的准则鼓励智能体将影响力聚焦于状态空间中探索不足的区域，同时利用资格迹使多个智能体在有益时能够持续对齐并维持对同一状态空间区域的影响力，从而促进协调且持久的联合行为。通过强调状态空间中探索不足的区域，FIM即使在极端稀疏奖励下也能实现更高效、结构化的探索。在多个多智能体强化学习基准测试中，FIM在合作性能上持续优于强基线方法。
Summary / 总结
Cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning under sparse rewards is challenging due to agents' inability to concentrate influence, resulting in poor coordination. The Focusing Influence Mechanism (FIM) addresses this by using an entropy-based criterion to direct agents toward under-explored state regions and employing eligibility traces to sustain coordinated influence. Experiments on diverse MARL benchmarks show FIM consistently outperforms strong baselines in cooperative tasks.
稀疏奖励下的多智能体强化学习因智能体无法集中影响力而导致协调探索不足。聚焦影响力机制（FIM）通过熵准则引导智能体关注未充分探索的状态区域，并利用资格迹维持多智能体协调一致的影响力。在多个MARL基准测试中，FIM在合作任务上持续优于强基线方法。
On the Impact of Crossover in Many-Objective Optimization: A Runtime Analysis of NSGA-III
Authors: Andre Opris
Venue: IJCAI 2026
First: 2026-05-11T20:09:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T20:09:54+00:00
Comments: This paper appears at IJCAI 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In recent years, a theoretical understanding has rapidly advanced regarding how popular multi-objective evolutionary algorithms (MOEAs) can optimize many-objective problems. However, the benefits of using crossover in many-objective optimization are theoretically not understood, except for specifically designed benchmark functions tuned to particular crossover operators, and still lag significantly behind its practical use. In this paper, we build upon this line of research and present a theoretical runtime analysis of the widely used NSGA-III algorithm on the classical $m$-objective $m$-OneJumpZeroJump function ($m$-OJZJ for short). Our results demonstrate that NSGA-III with crossover optimizes $m$-OJZJ asymptotically faster than NSGA-III without crossover for any number $m$ of objectives for huge parameter regimes. We complement our analysis by providing a lower runtime bound on $4$-OJZJ when crossover is turned off.
中文标题/摘要
标题：关于交叉操作在多目标优化中影响的理论分析：NSGA-III的运行时间研究
近年来，关于流行多目标进化算法（MOEAs）如何优化多目标问题的理论理解取得了快速进展。然而，除了针对特定交叉算子设计的基准函数外，交叉操作在多目标优化中的优势在理论上尚未得到理解，且仍显著落后于其实践应用。本文延续这一研究方向，对经典$m$目标$m$-OneJumpZeroJump函数（简称$m$-OJZJ）上广泛使用的NSGA-III算法进行了理论运行时间分析。结果表明，在巨大参数范围内，对于任意目标数$m$，使用交叉的NSGA-III优化$m$-OJZJ的渐近速度比不使用交叉的NSGA-III更快。我们通过提供关闭交叉时$4$-OJZJ的下界运行时间来补充分析。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the theoretical benefits of crossover in many-objective optimization by analyzing the runtime of the NSGA-III algorithm on the classical m-objective m-OneJumpZeroJump (m-OJZJ) problem. The authors provide a rigorous runtime analysis comparing NSGA-III with and without crossover, motivated by the gap between the practical success of crossover and the lack of theoretical understanding. Their main experimental results show that NSGA-III with crossover asymptotically outperforms the version without crossover on m-OJZJ for any number of objectives m across large parameter regimes, and they further prove a lower runtime bound for the 4-OJZJ problem when crossover is disabled, confirming its critical role in efficiency.
本文通过分析NSGA-III算法在经典m目标m-OneJumpZeroJump（m-OJZJ）问题上的运行时间，从理论上研究了交叉操作在多目标优化中的优势。作者针对交叉操作在实际中成功应用但缺乏理论理解这一差距，提供了有无交叉的NSGA-III的严格运行时间分析。主要实验结果表明，在广泛的参数范围内，对于任意目标数m，使用交叉的NSGA-III在m-OJZJ问题上的渐近运行时间优于不使用交叉的版本，并且进一步证明了在禁用交叉时4-OJZJ问题的下界运行时间，从而确认了交叉在效率中的关键作用。
Learning density ratios in causal inference using Bregman-Riesz regression
Authors: Oliver J. Hines, Caleb H. Miles
First: 2025-10-17T18:10:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T19:01:21+00:00
Comments: Replication code is available from https://github.com/CI-NYC/densityratios
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The ratio of two probability density functions is a fundamental quantity that appears in many areas of statistics and machine learning, including causal inference, reinforcement learning, covariate shift, outlier detection, independence testing, importance sampling, and diffusion modeling. Naively estimating the numerator and denominator densities separately using, e.g., kernel density estimators, can lead to unstable performance and suffer from the curse of dimensionality as the number of covariates increases. For this reason, several methods have been developed for estimating the density ratio directly based on (a) Bregman divergences or (b) recasting the density ratio as the odds in a probabilistic classification model that predicts whether an observation is sampled from the numerator or denominator distribution. Additionally, the density ratio can be viewed as the Riesz representer of a continuous linear map, making it amenable to estimation via (c) minimization of the so-called Riesz loss, which was developed to learn the Riesz representer in the Riesz regression procedure in causal inference. In this paper we show that all three of these methods can be unified in a common framework, which we call Bregman--Riesz regression. We further show how data augmentation techniques can be used to apply density ratio learning methods to causal problems, where the numerator distribution typically represents an unobserved intervention. We show through simulations how the choice of Bregman divergence and data augmentation strategy can affect the performance of the resulting density ratio learner. A Python package is provided for researchers to apply Bregman--Riesz regression in practice using gradient boosting, neural networks, and kernel methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用Bregman-Riesz回归学习因果推断中的密度比
两个概率密度函数的比值是统计与机器学习多个领域中的基本量，包括因果推断、强化学习、协变量偏移、异常检测、独立性检验、重要性采样和扩散建模。分别使用核密度估计等方法单独估计分子和分母密度，可能导致性能不稳定，并随着协变量数量增加而遭受维度灾难。为此，已有多种方法直接估计密度比，基于：(a) Bregman散度，或(b)将密度比重述为概率分类模型中的优势比，该模型预测观测值来自分子分布还是分母分布。此外，密度比可视为连续线性映射的Riesz表示，因此可通过(c)最小化所谓的Riesz损失进行估计——该方法最初为在因果推断的Riesz回归过程中学习Riesz表示而开发。本文表明，这三种方法均可统一于一个共同框架，我们称之为Bregman-Riesz回归。我们进一步展示了如何利用数据增强技术将密度比学习方法应用于因果问题，其中分子分布通常代表未观测的干预。通过模拟实验，我们展示了Bregman散度的选择和数据增强策略如何影响所得密度比学习器的性能。我们提供了一个Python包，供研究人员在实践中使用梯度提升、神经网络和核方法应用Bregman-Riesz回归。
Summary / 总结
This paper unifies three existing approaches for density ratio estimation—Bregman divergence minimization, probabilistic classification, and Riesz representer learning—into a single framework called Bregman-Riesz regression. The method directly estimates the ratio of two probability densities without separately modeling each density, addressing the curse of dimensionality in high-dimensional covariate spaces. The authors further incorporate data augmentation techniques to adapt density ratio learning to causal inference problems where the numerator distribution corresponds to an unobserved intervention. Simulation results demonstrate that the choice of Bregman divergence and data augmentation strategy significantly impacts the performance of the density ratio learner, with the provided Python package enabling practical application via gradient boosting, neural networks, and kernel methods.
本文将密度比估计的三种现有方法——Bregman散度最小化、概率分类和Riesz表示学习——统一到一个称为Bregman-Riesz回归的框架中。该方法直接估计两个概率密度的比值，无需分别建模每个密度，从而解决了高维协变量空间中的维度灾难问题。作者进一步引入数据增强技术，将密度比学习应用于因果推断问题，其中分子分布对应未观测的干预。模拟结果表明，Bregman散度和数据增强策略的选择会显著影响密度比学习器的性能，提供的Python包支持通过梯度提升、神经网络和核方法进行实际应用。
RankQ: Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning via Self-Supervised Action Ranking
Authors: Andrew Choi, Wei Xu
First: 2026-05-11T18:58:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T18:58:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline-to-online reinforcement learning (RL) improves sample efficiency by leveraging pre-collected datasets prior to online interaction. A key challenge, however, is learning an accurate critic in large state--action spaces with limited dataset coverage. To mitigate harmful updates from value overestimation, prior methods impose pessimism by down-weighting out-of-distribution (OOD) actions relative to dataset actions. While effective, this essentially acts as a behavior cloning anchor and can hinder downstream online policy improvement when dataset actions are suboptimal. We propose RankQ, an offline-to-online Q-learning objective that augments temporal-difference learning with a self-supervised multi-term ranking loss to enforce structured action ordering. By learning relative action preferences rather than uniformly penalizing unseen actions, RankQ shapes the Q-function such that action gradients are directed toward higher-quality behaviors. Across sparse reward D4RL benchmarks, RankQ achieves performance competitive with or superior to seven prior methods. In vision-based robot learning, RankQ enables effective offline-to-online fine-tuning of a pretrained vision-language-action (VLA) model in a low-data regime, achieving on average a 42.7% higher simulation success rate than the next best method. In a high-data setting, RankQ improves simulation performance by 13.7% over the next best method and achieves strong sim-to-real transfer, increasing real-world cube stacking success from 43.1% to 84.7% relative to the VLA's initial performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RankQ：通过自监督动作排序实现离线到在线强化学习
离线到在线强化学习通过利用在线交互前收集的预训练数据集来提高样本效率。然而，一个关键挑战是在数据集覆盖有限的大状态-动作空间中学习准确的评论家。为了减轻价值高估带来的有害更新，先前的方法通过降低分布外动作相对于数据集动作的权重来施加悲观主义。虽然有效，但这本质上充当了行为克隆锚点，当数据集动作次优时可能阻碍后续在线策略改进。我们提出RankQ，一种离线到在线的Q学习目标，通过自监督多项排序损失增强时序差分学习，以强制执行结构化动作排序。通过学习相对动作偏好而非统一惩罚未见动作，RankQ塑造Q函数，使动作梯度指向更高质量的行为。在稀疏奖励D4RL基准测试中，RankQ实现了与七种先前方法竞争或更优的性能。在基于视觉的机器人学习中，RankQ在低数据场景下实现了预训练视觉-语言-动作模型的有效离线到在线微调，平均模拟成功率比次优方法高42.7%。在高数据场景下，RankQ将模拟性能比次优方法提升13.7%，并实现了强大的模拟到现实迁移，将真实世界立方体堆叠成功率从VLA初始性能的43.1%提升至84.7%。
Summary / 总结
RankQ addresses the challenge of offline-to-online reinforcement learning where limited dataset coverage leads to value overestimation and suboptimal policy improvement. The method introduces a self-supervised multi-term ranking loss that augments temporal-difference learning, enforcing structured action ordering to shape the Q-function toward higher-quality behaviors instead of uniformly penalizing unseen actions. Experiments on D4RL benchmarks show RankQ achieves competitive or superior performance to seven prior methods, while in vision-based robot learning it improves simulation success rates by 42.7% in low-data regimes and 13.7% in high-data settings, with real-world cube stacking success increasing from 43.1% to 84.7%.
RankQ针对离线到在线强化学习中数据集覆盖有限导致的价值高估和策略改进受阻问题，提出了一种自监督多术语排序损失来增强时序差分学习，通过强制动作的结构化排序来塑造Q函数，使其偏向更高质量的行为，而非统一惩罚未见动作。在D4RL基准测试中，RankQ的性能与七种先前方法相当或更优；在基于视觉的机器人学习中，低数据场景下模拟成功率平均提升42.7%，高数据场景下提升13.7%，真实世界叠方块成功率从43.1%提升至84.7%。
DARLING: Detection Augmented Reinforcement Learning with Non-Stationary Guarantees
Authors: Argyrios Gerogiannis, Yu-Han Huang, Venugopal V. Veeravalli
First: 2026-04-17T20:41:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T18:31:11+00:00
Comments: 50 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study model-free reinforcement learning (RL) in non-stationary finite-horizon episodic Markov decision processes (MDPs) without prior knowledge of the non-stationarity. We focus on the piecewise stationary (PS) setting, where both rewards and transition dynamics can change at unknown times. We first revisit existing state-of-the-art approaches and identify theoretical and practical limitations that change the current landscape of performance guarantees. To characterize the difficulty of the problem, we establish the first minimax lower bounds for PS-RL in tabular and linear MDPs. We then introduce Detection Augmented Reinforcement Learning (DARLING), a modular wrapper for PS-RL that applies to both tabular and linear MDPs, without knowledge of the changes. In tabular MDPs, under change-point separability and reachability conditions, DARLING improves the best known dynamic regret bounds and matches our minimax lower bound. In linear MDPs, DARLING matches the minimax lower bound when the relevant reachability parameters are known, and our analysis clarifies the structural obstacles that distinguish this setting from the tabular case. Finally, through extensive experimentation across diverse non-stationary benchmarks, we show that DARLING consistently surpasses the state-of-the-art methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DARLING：具有非平稳性保证的检测增强强化学习
我们研究了在非平稳有限时域情节马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）中，无需事先了解非平稳性的无模型强化学习（RL）。我们专注于分段平稳（PS）设置，其中奖励和转移动态均可在未知时间发生变化。我们首先重新审视现有最先进的方法，并识别出改变当前性能保证格局的理论和实践局限性。为了刻画问题的难度，我们在表格型和线性MDP中建立了PS-RL的首个极小化极大下界。随后，我们引入了检测增强强化学习（DARLING），这是一种适用于PS-RL的模块化包装器，可应用于表格型和线性MDP，且无需了解变化点。在表格型MDP中，在变化点可分离性和可达性条件下，DARLING改进了已知的动态遗憾界，并匹配了我们的极小化极大下界。在线性MDP中，当相关可达性参数已知时，DARLING匹配了极小化极大下界，而我们的分析阐明了区分该设置与表格型情况的结构性障碍。最后，通过在多样化的非平稳基准上进行广泛实验，我们展示了DARLING持续超越最先进的方法。
Summary / 总结
This paper studies model-free reinforcement learning in non-stationary episodic MDPs without prior knowledge of changes, focusing on the piecewise stationary setting where both rewards and transitions shift at unknown times. The authors first identify limitations in existing approaches and establish the first minimax lower bounds for PS-RL in tabular and linear MDPs. They then propose DARLING, a modular detection-augmented wrapper that works for both settings without change knowledge. In tabular MDPs, under separability and reachability conditions, DARLING improves the best known dynamic regret bounds and matches the minimax lower bound; in linear MDPs, it matches the lower bound when reachability parameters are known. Extensive experiments on diverse non-stationary benchmarks show DARLING consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods.
本文研究在无先验变化知识的情况下，非平稳有限时域情节马尔可夫决策过程中的无模型强化学习，重点关注奖励和转移动态均在未知时间发生变化的片段平稳设定。作者首先指出现有方法的局限性，并为表格型和线性MDP中的PS-RL建立了首个极小极大下界。随后提出DARLING，一种模块化的检测增强包装器，无需变化知识即可适用于两种设定。在表格型MDP中，在可分离性和可达性条件下，DARLING改进了已知的最佳动态遗憾界并匹配极小极大下界；在线性MDP中，当相关可达性参数已知时，它匹配极小极大下界。在多种非平稳基准上的大量实验表明，DARLING始终优于现有最先进方法。
Newton's Lantern: A Reinforcement Learning Framework for Finetuning AC Power Flow Warm Start Models
Authors: Shourya Bose, Helgi Hilmarsson, Dhruv Suri
First: 2026-05-11T18:06:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T18:06:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural warm starts can sharply reduce the number of Newton-Raphson iterations required to solve the AC power flow problem, but existing supervised approaches generalize poorly on heavily loaded instances near voltage collapse. We prove a lower bound on the Newton-Raphson iteration count that depends on the direction of the warm start error rather than on its magnitude, and show as a corollary that the bound becomes vacuous as the smallest singular value of the power-flow Jacobian shrinks, identifying the failure mode of supervised regression near the saddle-node bifurcation. Motivated by this analysis, we introduce Newton's Lantern, a finetuning pipeline that combines group relative policy optimization with a learned reward model trained on perturbations of the base model's predictions, using the iteration count itself as the supervisory signal. Across IEEE 118-bus, GOC 500-bus, and GOC 2000-bus benchmarks, Newton's Lantern is the only method that converges on every test snapshot while attaining the smallest mean iteration count.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the poor generalization of supervised neural warm starts for AC power flow solvers under heavily loaded conditions near voltage collapse. The authors prove a lower bound on Newton-Raphson iterations dependent on the error direction rather than magnitude, revealing that the bound becomes vacuous near saddle-node bifurcations due to small Jacobian singular values. To overcome this, they propose Newton's Lantern, a reinforcement learning finetuning framework using group relative policy optimization and a learned reward model trained on perturbed predictions, with iteration count as the reward signal. Experiments on IEEE 118-bus, GOC 500-bus, and GOC 2000-bus benchmarks show that Newton's Lantern uniquely converges on all test snapshots while achieving the smallest mean iteration count.
该论文针对现有监督式神经暖启动方法在重载接近电压崩溃场景下泛化能力差的问题展开研究。作者证明了牛顿-拉夫逊迭代次数的下界取决于误差方向而非幅度，并指出在鞍结分岔点附近因雅可比矩阵最小奇异值变小而导致该下界失效。为此，他们提出牛顿灯笼框架，通过结合群体相对策略优化和基于扰动预测训练的学习奖励模型，以迭代次数作为监督信号进行微调。在IEEE 118节点、GOC 500节点和GOC 2000节点基准测试中，牛顿灯笼是唯一能在所有测试快照上收敛且获得最小平均迭代次数的方法。
Dynamic Skill Lifecycle Management for Agentic Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Junhao Shen, Teng Zhang, Xiaoyan Zhao, Hong Cheng
First: 2026-05-11T17:55:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T17:55:13+00:00
Comments: Implementation code is available at https://github.com/ejhshen/SLIM
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language model agents increasingly rely on external skills to solve complex tasks, where skills act as modular units that extend their capabilities beyond what parametric memory alone supports. Existing methods assume external skills either accumulate as persistent guidance or internalized into the policy, eventually leading to zero-skill inference. We argue this assumption is overly restrictive, since with limited parametric capacity and uneven marginal contribution across skills, the optimal active skill set is non-monotonic, task- and stage-dependent. In this work, we propose SLIM, a framework of dynamic Skill LIfecycle Management for agentic reinforcement learning (RL), which treats the active external skill set as a dynamic optimization variable jointly updated with policy learning. Specifically, SLIM estimates each active skill's marginal external contribution through leave-one-skill-out validation, then applies three lifecycle operations: retaining high-value skills, retiring skills whose contribution becomes negligible after sufficient exposure, and expanding the skill bank when persistent failures reveal missing capability coverage. Experiments show that SLIM outperforms the best baselines by an average of 7.1% points across ALFWorld and SearchQA. Results further indicate that policy learning and external skill retention are not mutually exclusive: some skills are absorbed into the policy, while others continue to provide external value, supporting SLIM as a more general paradigm for skill-based agentic RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向智能体强化学习的动态技能生命周期管理
大语言模型智能体日益依赖外部技能来解决复杂任务，其中技能作为模块化单元，扩展了其超越参数化记忆支持的能力。现有方法假设外部技能要么作为持久指导积累，要么内化到策略中，最终导致零技能推理。我们认为这一假设过于严格，因为受限于有限的参数容量和技能间不均衡的边际贡献，最优活跃技能集是非单调的、依赖于任务和阶段的。本文提出SLIM框架，一种面向智能体强化学习的动态技能生命周期管理方法，将活跃外部技能集视为与策略学习联合更新的动态优化变量。具体而言，SLIM通过留一技能验证估计每个活跃技能的边际外部贡献，然后应用三种生命周期操作：保留高价值技能、在充分暴露后贡献可忽略时淘汰技能、以及在持续失败揭示缺失能力覆盖时扩展技能库。实验表明，在ALFWorld和SearchQA上，SLIM平均比最佳基线高出7.1个百分点。结果进一步表明，策略学习与外部技能保留并非互斥：部分技能被吸收到策略中，而其他技能继续提供外部价值，支持SLIM作为基于技能的智能体强化学习更通用的范式。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of existing methods that assume external skills for large language model agents either accumulate persistently or are fully internalized, leading to zero-skill inference, which is restrictive given limited parametric capacity and uneven skill contributions. The authors propose SLIM, a dynamic Skill Lifecycle Management framework for agentic reinforcement learning that treats the active external skill set as a dynamic optimization variable, using leave-one-skill-out validation to estimate marginal contributions and applying lifecycle operations like retaining high-value skills, retiring negligible ones, and expanding the bank when failures indicate missing coverage. Experiments on ALFWorld and SearchQA show SLIM outperforms baselines by an average of 7.1% points, demonstrating that policy learning and external skill retention can coexist, with some skills absorbed and others providing ongoing external value.
该论文指出现有方法假设大型语言模型代理的外部技能要么持续积累要么完全内化，最终导致零技能推理，这种假设过于严格，因为参数容量有限且技能边际贡献不均。作者提出SLIM，一个用于代理强化学习的动态技能生命周期管理框架，将外部技能集视为动态优化变量，通过留一技能验证估计边际贡献，并应用保留高价值技能、淘汰贡献可忽略的技能以及在失败揭示能力缺失时扩展技能库等生命周期操作。在ALFWorld和SearchQA上的实验表明，SLIM平均比最佳基线高出7.1个百分点，证明策略学习与外部技能保留并非互斥，部分技能被内化而其他技能持续提供外部价值。
Equivariant Reinforcement Learning for Clifford Quantum Circuit Synthesis
Authors: Richie Yeung, Aleks Kissinger, Rob Cornish
First: 2026-05-11T17:49:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T17:49:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We consider the problem of synthesizing Clifford quantum circuits for devices with all-to-all qubit connectivity. We approach this task as a reinforcement learning problem in which an agent learns to discover a sequence of elementary Clifford gates that reduces a given symplectic matrix representation of a Clifford circuit to the identity. This formulation permits a simple learning curriculum based on random walks from the identity. We introduce a novel neural network architecture that is equivariant to qubit relabelings of the symplectic matrix representation, and which is size-agnostic, allowing a single learned policy to be applied across different qubit counts without circuit splicing or network reparameterization. On six-qubit Clifford circuits, the largest regime for which optimal references are available, our agent finds circuits within one two-qubit gate of optimality in milliseconds per instance, and finds optimal circuits in 99.2% of instances within seconds per instance. After continued training on ten-qubit instances, the agent scales to unseen Clifford tableaus with up to thirty qubits, including targets generated from circuits with over a thousand Clifford gates, where it achieves lower average two-qubit gate counts than Qiskit's Aaronson-Gottesman and greedy Clifford synthesizers.
Summary / 总结
This work tackles Clifford quantum circuit synthesis for all-to-all connected devices using reinforcement learning, where an agent learns to reduce a symplectic matrix representation of a Clifford circuit to the identity via elementary gates. The method introduces a novel neural network architecture that is equivariant to qubit relabelings and size-agnostic, enabling a single policy to handle varying qubit counts without reparameterization. On six-qubit circuits, the agent achieves near-optimal results within milliseconds per instance and finds optimal circuits in 99.2% of cases within seconds, while scaling to thirty-qubit instances it outperforms Qiskit's synthesizers in reducing two-qubit gate counts.
该工作针对全连接量子设备上的克利福德电路综合问题，采用强化学习方法，让智能体学习通过基本门操作将克利福德电路的辛矩阵表示约化为单位矩阵。方法提出了一种新颖的神经网络架构，该架构对量子比特重标号具有等变性且与规模无关，使得单一策略无需重新参数化即可适用于不同量子比特数。在六量子比特电路上，智能体在毫秒级时间内达到接近最优结果，并在99.2%的实例中于数秒内找到最优电路；扩展到三十量子比特时，其在双量子比特门数量上优于Qiskit的合成器。
Distributionally Robust Token Optimization in RLHF
Authors: Yeping Jin, Jiaming Hu, Ioannis Ch. Paschalidis
First: 2026-03-27T21:36:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T17:42:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) tend to respond correctly to prompts that align well with the data they were trained and fine-tuned on. Yet, small shifts in wording, format, or language can trigger surprisingly large failures, especially on multi-step reasoning problems. To address this problem, we propose a Distributionally Robust Token Optimization (DRTO) approach, which combines token-level Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) with Distributionally Robust Optimization (DRO). DRTO constructs f-divergence ambiguity sets over span-level actor losses, providing a principled way to emphasize difficult response segments during policy optimization. Empirically, DRTO enhances consistency under distribution shifts in multiple reasoning benchmarks among different tasks, achieving $+4.4$ percentage points on MATH-500 and $+2.7$ percentage points on LiveCodeBench over standard RTO.
Summary / 总结
Large Language Models often fail on reasoning tasks when faced with slight distribution shifts in prompts. To address this, the authors propose Distributionally Robust Token Optimization (DRTO), which integrates token-level Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback with Distributionally Robust Optimization by constructing f-divergence ambiguity sets over span-level actor losses to emphasize difficult response segments during policy optimization. Empirically, DRTO improves consistency under distribution shifts, achieving a +4.4 percentage point gain on MATH-500 and a +2.7 percentage point gain on LiveCodeBench over standard RTO.
大型语言模型在面对提示词的微小分布偏移时，常在推理任务上出现严重失败。为此，作者提出分布鲁棒令牌优化方法，将令牌级人类反馈强化学习与分布鲁棒优化相结合，通过构建跨度级演员损失的f-散度模糊集，在策略优化中强调困难响应片段。实验表明，该方法增强了分布偏移下的一致性，在MATH-500和LiveCodeBench上分别比标准RTO提升了4.4和2.7个百分点。
RubricEM: Meta-RL with Rubric-guided Policy Decomposition beyond Verifiable Rewards
Authors: Gaotang Li, Bhavana Dalvi Mishra, Zifeng Wang, Jun Yan, Yanfei Chen, Chun-Liang Li, Long T. Le, Rujun Han, George Lee, Hanghang Tong, Chen-Yu Lee, Tomas Pfister
First: 2026-05-11T17:40:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T17:40:38+00:00
Comments: 63 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Training deep research agents, namely systems that plan, search, evaluate evidence, and synthesize long-form reports, pushes reinforcement learning beyond the regime of verifiable rewards. Their outputs lack ground-truth answers, their trajectories span many tool-augmented decisions, and standard post-training offers little mechanism for turning past attempts into reusable experience. In this work, we argue that rubrics should serve not merely as final-answer evaluators, but as the shared interface that structures policy execution, judge feedback, and agent memory. Based on this view, we introduce RubricEM, a rubric-guided reinforcement learning framework that combines stagewise policy decomposition with reflection-based meta-policy evolution. RubricEM first makes research trajectories stage-aware by conditioning planning, evidence gathering, review, and synthesis on self-generated rubrics. It then assigns credit with Stage-Structured GRPO, which uses stagewise rubric judgments to provide denser semantic feedback for long-horizon optimization. In parallel, RubricEM trains a shared-backbone reflection meta-policy that distills judged trajectories into reusable rubric-grounded guidance for future attempts. The resulting RubricEM-8B achieves strong performance across four long-form research benchmarks, outperforming comparable open models and approaching proprietary deep-research systems. Beyond final performance, we perform thorough analyses to understand the key ingredients of RubricEM.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RubricEM：超越可验证奖励的元强化学习与评分准则引导的策略分解
训练深度研究智能体——即能够规划、搜索、评估证据并综合生成长篇报告的系统——将强化学习推向了可验证奖励的范畴之外。它们的输出缺乏标准答案，其轨迹涉及众多工具增强的决策，而标准的后训练过程几乎无法将过去的尝试转化为可复用的经验。在这项工作中，我们认为评分准则不应仅仅作为最终答案的评估器，而应作为结构化策略执行、评判反馈和智能体记忆的共享接口。基于这一观点，我们引入了RubricEM，一个评分准则引导的强化学习框架，它将分阶段策略分解与基于反思的元策略演化相结合。RubricEM首先通过让规划、证据收集、审查和综合依赖于自生成的评分准则，使研究轨迹具有阶段感知能力。然后，它使用阶段结构化的GRPO进行信用分配，该机制利用分阶段的评分准则判断为长程优化提供更密集的语义反馈。同时，RubricEM训练一个共享骨干网络的反思元策略，将经过评判的轨迹提炼为可复用的、基于评分准则的指导，用于未来的尝试。由此产生的RubricEM-8B在四个长篇研究基准测试中取得了强劲的性能，超越了同类开源模型，并接近专有的深度研究系统。除了最终性能外，我们还进行了深入分析以理解RubricEM的关键要素。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of training deep research agents in reinforcement learning where verifiable rewards are unavailable due to the complexity of long-form outputs and tool-augmented trajectories. The authors propose RubricEM, a framework that uses rubrics not just for evaluation but as a shared interface to structure policy execution, judge feedback, and agent memory. It decomposes policies into stagewise components (planning, evidence gathering, review, synthesis) conditioned on self-generated rubrics, employs Stage-Structured GRPO for denser semantic credit assignment, and trains a reflection meta-policy to distill past experiences into reusable guidance. Experiments on four long-form research benchmarks show that RubricEM-8B outperforms comparable open models and approaches proprietary deep-research systems, with thorough analyses confirming the effectiveness of its key components.
该论文针对深度研究智能体在强化学习中因输出缺乏标准答案、轨迹复杂而无法使用可验证奖励的问题，提出RubricEM框架。该框架将评分标准不仅作为最终评估工具，更作为结构化策略执行、评判反馈和智能体记忆的共享接口。它通过自生成评分标准将策略分解为规划、证据收集、审查和合成等阶段，利用阶段结构化GRPO提供更密集的语义信用分配，并训练反思元策略将评判过的轨迹提炼为可复用的指导。在四个长程研究基准测试中，RubricEM-8B模型表现优于同类开源模型，接近专有深度研究系统，详细分析验证了其关键组件的有效性。
Reinforcement Learning with Action Chunking
Authors: Qiyang Li, Zhiyuan Zhou, Sergey Levine
Venue: NeurIPS 2025
First: 2025-07-10T17:48:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T17:12:21+00:00
Comments: The Thirty-Ninth Annual Conference on Neural Information Processing Systems (NeurIPS 2025); 29 pages, 17 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present Q-chunking, a simple yet effective recipe for improving reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms for long-horizon, sparse-reward tasks. Our recipe is designed for the offline-to-online RL setting, where the goal is to leverage an offline prior dataset to maximize the sample-efficiency of online learning. Effective exploration and sample-efficient learning remain central challenges in this setting, as it is not obvious how the offline data should be utilized to acquire a good exploratory policy. Our key insight is that action chunking, a technique popularized in imitation learning where sequences of future actions are predicted rather than a single action at each timestep, can be applied to temporal difference (TD)-based RL methods to mitigate the exploration challenge. Q-chunking adopts action chunking by directly running RL in a 'chunked' action space, enabling the agent to (1) leverage temporally consistent behaviors from offline data for more effective online exploration and (2) use unbiased $n$-step backups for more stable and efficient TD learning. Our experimental results demonstrate that Q-chunking exhibits strong offline performance and online sample efficiency, outperforming prior best offline-to-online methods on a range of long-horizon, sparse-reward manipulation tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于动作分块的强化学习
我们提出Q-chunking，一种简单而有效的改进强化学习算法的方法，适用于长时域、稀疏奖励任务。该方法专为离线到在线强化学习场景设计，旨在利用离线先验数据集最大化在线学习的样本效率。在此场景中，有效探索和样本高效学习仍是核心挑战，因为如何利用离线数据获取良好的探索策略并不明确。我们的关键见解是，动作分块（一种在模仿学习中流行的技术，即预测未来动作序列而非单步动作）可应用于基于时序差分的强化学习方法，以缓解探索难题。Q-chunking通过直接在“分块”动作空间中运行强化学习来采用动作分块，使智能体能够：(1) 利用离线数据中的时序一致行为进行更有效的在线探索，(2) 使用无偏的n步回溯实现更稳定高效的时序差分学习。实验结果表明，Q-chunking在离线性能和在线样本效率上均表现优异，在多项长时域、稀疏奖励操作任务中超越了先前最优的离线到在线方法。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Q-chunking, a method to improve reinforcement learning for long-horizon, sparse-reward tasks in the offline-to-online setting, where leveraging offline data for sample-efficient online learning is challenging. The key idea is to apply action chunking, which predicts sequences of future actions instead of a single action, to temporal difference-based RL by operating in a chunked action space. This enables temporally consistent behaviors from offline data for better exploration and unbiased n-step backups for stable learning. Experiments show Q-chunking achieves strong offline performance and online sample efficiency, outperforming prior methods on various manipulation tasks.
该论文提出了Q-chunking方法，旨在改进离线到在线强化学习场景中长视野、稀疏奖励任务的性能，该场景下如何利用离线数据实现高效的在线学习仍是一大挑战。核心思路是将模仿学习中流行的动作分块技术应用于基于时序差分的强化学习，通过在分块动作空间中直接运行RL，使智能体能利用离线数据中的时间一致行为进行更有效的在线探索，并使用无偏的n步回溯实现更稳定的学习。实验结果表明，Q-chunking在多种长视野、稀疏奖励的操控任务中展现出强大的离线性能和在线样本效率，优于先前的最佳方法。
